   function getCookie(name) { for (var nameEQ = name + "=", ca = document.cookie.split(";"), i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) { for (var c = ca[i]; " " == c.charAt(0);)c = c.substring(1, c.length); if (0 == c.indexOf(nameEQ)) return c.substring(nameEQ.length, c.length) } return null }            
            function setCookie(name,value,days) {var expires = ""; if (days) {var date = new Date();date.setTime(date.getTime() + (days*24*60*60*1000)); expires = "; expires=" + date.toUTCString();} document.cookie = name + "=" + (value || "")  + expires + "; path=/" + ";domain=.macrumors.com";}
            function eraseCookie(name) {document.cookie = name+'=; Max-Age=-99999999;'+'; path=/' + ';domain=.macrumors.com';}

              <img alt="iphone 12 red color fading" class="lazyload" data-sizes="auto" data-src="https://images.macrumors.com/t/NipGTd6-CnjANnkhy6atenWSjT8=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/iphone-12-red-color-fading.jpg?lossy" data-srcset="https://images.macrumors.com/t/NipGTd6-CnjANnkhy6atenWSjT8=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/iphone-12-red-color-fading.jpg?lossy 400w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/LBfVoaXH8KvTlxoLJWII3DHnImE=/800x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/iphone-12-red-color-fading.jpg?lossy 800w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/zUQ3byz-MAvj8ToAGM1wgKAfRTE=/1600x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/iphone-12-red-color-fading.jpg 1600w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/nSbuWtXQL1D-ka4zJ51-WNk4obw=/2500x0/filters:no_upscale():quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/iphone-12-red-color-fading.jpg 2500w" src="https://images.macrumors.com/images-new/1x1.trans.gif"/>

               <img alt="iphone 12 red color fading" sizes="(max-width: 610px) 100vw, (max-width:900px) 33vw, 25vw" src="https://images.macrumors.com/t/NipGTd6-CnjANnkhy6atenWSjT8=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/iphone-12-red-color-fading.jpg?lossy" srcset="https://images.macrumors.com/t/NipGTd6-CnjANnkhy6atenWSjT8=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/iphone-12-red-color-fading.jpg?lossy 400w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/LBfVoaXH8KvTlxoLJWII3DHnImE=/800x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/iphone-12-red-color-fading.jpg?lossy 800w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/zUQ3byz-MAvj8ToAGM1wgKAfRTE=/1600x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/iphone-12-red-color-fading.jpg 1600w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/nSbuWtXQL1D-ka4zJ51-WNk4obw=/2500x0/filters:no_upscale():quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/iphone-12-red-color-fading.jpg 2500w"/>

       <article class="article--2pJwZBkO js-article front--3uTQDaAu f_front" expanded="false">
        <div class="titlebar--3N4MCKxL">
         <h2 class="heading--1cooZo6n heading--h5--3l5xQ3lN heading--white--2vAPsAl1 heading--noMargin--mnRHPAnD">
          <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/20/512gb-1tb-ssd-imac-21-discontinued/">
           Apple Discontinues 512GB and 1TB SSD Configurations of 4K 21.5-inch iMac
          </a>
         </h2>
        </div>
        <div class="byline--3Eec5bcq">
         <time datetime="2021-03-20T08:15:58-07:00">
          Saturday March 20, 2021 8:15 am PDT
         </time>
         by
         <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/author/sami-fathi/" rel="author">
          Sami Fathi
         </a>
        </div>
        <div class="content--2u3grYDr js-content">
         <div class="ugc--2nTu61bm minor--3O_9dH4U" data-io-article-url="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/20/512gb-1tb-ssd-imac-21-discontinued/">
          <div class="js-contentInner">
           <p>
            Just hours after
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/19/imac-pro-officially-discontinued/">
             officially discontinuing the iMac Pro
            </a>
            , Apple has also discontinued the 512GB and 1TB SSD configurations of the 4K 21.5-inch
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/roundup/imac/">
             iMac
            </a>
            .
           </p>
           <p>
            <img alt="imac 21 ssds discontinued" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-790010 lazyload" data-sizes="auto" data-src="https://images.macrumors.com/t/tonZ4wHfu8fJVcTbwo2lL4khc1E=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/imac-21-ssds-discontinued.jpg?lossy" data-srcset="https://images.macrumors.com/t/tonZ4wHfu8fJVcTbwo2lL4khc1E=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/imac-21-ssds-discontinued.jpg?lossy 400w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/cn_VsqaMOGKCJcejTzIGBEIJDjE=/800x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/imac-21-ssds-discontinued.jpg?lossy 800w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/tkaVCr_H6QVT7KnIQLRSxS_twhg=/1600x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/imac-21-ssds-discontinued.jpg 1600w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/KFoaBZbMGdFBnn_vsVJruqJ15uA=/2500x0/filters:no_upscale():quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/imac-21-ssds-discontinued.jpg 2500w" height="657" src="https://images.macrumors.com/images-new/1x1.trans.gif" width="1600"/>
            <noscript>
             <img alt="imac 21 ssds discontinued" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-790010" height="657" src="https://images.macrumors.com/article-new/2021/03/imac-21-ssds-discontinued.jpg" width="1600"/>
            </noscript>
            <br/>
            Last month, both options
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/02/25/21-5-inch-imac-ssd-upgrades-unavailable/">
             became unavailable for purchase
            </a>
            , although it was unclear at the time whether it was a temporary issue due to a component supply problem or if it was a permanent decision to no longer offer the options.
           </p>
           <p>
            Apple has now removed both of the affected SSD options from the iMacs configuration page entirely, leaving a 256GB SSD and a 1TB Fusion Drive as the only options for customers.
           </p>
           <p>
            An
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/01/15/apple-redesigned-imacs-slimmer-bezels/">
             all-new redesigned iMac
            </a>
            based on Apple silicon is expected to launch later this year, but a more specific launch timeframe isn't yet known.
           </p>
           <div class="linkback">
            Related Roundup:
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/roundup/imac/">
             iMac
            </a>
           </div>
           <div class="linkback">
            Buyer's Guide:
            <a href="https://buyersguide.macrumors.com/#iMac">
             iMac (Caution)
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>

       <article class="article--2pJwZBkO js-article front--3uTQDaAu f_front" expanded="false">
        <div class="titlebar--3N4MCKxL">
         <h2 class="heading--1cooZo6n heading--h5--3l5xQ3lN heading--white--2vAPsAl1 heading--noMargin--mnRHPAnD">
          <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/20/apple-brazil-fine-iphone-charger/">
           Apple Fined $2 Million in Brazil for Selling iPhones Without Chargers
          </a>
         </h2>
        </div>
        <div class="byline--3Eec5bcq">
         <time datetime="2021-03-20T08:04:32-07:00">
          Saturday March 20, 2021 8:04 am PDT
         </time>
         by
         <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/author/sami-fathi/" rel="author">
          Sami Fathi
         </a>
        </div>
        <div class="content--2u3grYDr js-content">
         <div class="ugc--2nTu61bm minor--3O_9dH4U" data-io-article-url="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/20/apple-brazil-fine-iphone-charger/">
          <div class="js-contentInner">
           <p>
            Apple has been slapped with a near $2 million fine in the Brazilian state of So Paulo over violations of the Consumer Law Code due to the lack of a charger in the box for newer iPhones, Brazilian tech news outlet
            <em>
             <a href="https://www.uol.com.br/tilt/noticias/redacao/2021/03/19/procon-sp-multa-apple-em-r-10-milhoes-por-vender-iphone-sem-carregador.htm">
              Tilt
             </a>
            </em>
            reports.
           </p>
           <p>
            <img alt="iphone 11 pro charger" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-756595 lazyload" data-sizes="auto" data-src="https://images.macrumors.com/t/3YylHbqvzsBDHqVW0lcv-x5yNBE=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2020/08/iphone-11-pro-charger.jpg?lossy" data-srcset="https://images.macrumors.com/t/3YylHbqvzsBDHqVW0lcv-x5yNBE=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2020/08/iphone-11-pro-charger.jpg?lossy 400w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/d8guUVxizJ4ScAdypDgY0RSOo7o=/800x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2020/08/iphone-11-pro-charger.jpg?lossy 800w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/M4fowHM9qII6rB9Iusl54MBtk94=/1600x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2020/08/iphone-11-pro-charger.jpg 1600w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/YwdSlB-0YZFquQklBmdg8F5l2aA=/2500x0/filters:no_upscale():quality(90)/article-new/2020/08/iphone-11-pro-charger.jpg 2500w" height="1038" src="https://images.macrumors.com/images-new/1x1.trans.gif" width="1600"/>
            <noscript>
             <img alt="iphone 11 pro charger" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-756595" height="1038" src="https://images.macrumors.com/article-new/2020/08/iphone-11-pro-charger.jpg" width="1600"/>
            </noscript>
            <br/>
            Procon-SP, So Paulo's consumer protection agency, decided to fine Apple following intense scrutiny over the decision to remove the power adapter from the boxes of iPhones. With the
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/roundup/iphone-12/">
             iPhone 12
            </a>
            , Apple removed the power adapter from the box, saying that doing so will reduce carbon emissions and the use of rare-earth metals.
           </p>
           <p>
            In December, the Brazilian agency
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2020/12/03/apple-may-have-to-include-charger-iphone-brazil/">
             informed Apple
            </a>
            that selling an
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/guide/iphone/">
             iPhone
            </a>
            in the country without a charger in the box is a violation of the Consumer Defense Code. Apple responded to the agency's concerns by saying that most customers already have spare adapters and that providing another one in the box is unneeded.
           </p>
           <p>
            Fernando Capez, Procon-SP's executive director, offered a stern warning to Apple following the fine, saying that it needs to respect and understand Brazilian consumer law and institutions. Alongside the lack of a charger, Apple is also being fined for misleading customers about the water resistance in iPhones.
           </p>
           <p>
            Since the iPhone 7, iPhones have been water-resistant to different specifications. The more recent iPhone 12 series, for example, is certified for water submersion of up to 6 meters for as long as 30 minutes.
           </p>
           <p>
            Procon-SP claims that Apple refused to repair devices for customers who had suffered water damage with their "water-resistant" iPhones, even though they're under warranty. Other charges brought forward to Apple are claims that it
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/01/iphone-lawsuit-programmed-obsolescence-portugal/">
             deliberately slows down
            </a>
            older phones with iOS updates to encourage customers to purchase newer models.
           </p>
           <p>
            Apple will have a chance to appeal to the $2 million fine. We've reached out to Apple for comment and will update this article if we hear back.
           </p>
           <div class="linkback">
            Tag:
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/guide/brazil/">
             Brazil
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>

           </a>
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>

           <div class="tShare--2sClpP_C">

       <article class="article--2pJwZBkO js-article front--3uTQDaAu f_front" expanded="false">
        <div class="titlebar--3N4MCKxL">
         <h2 class="heading--1cooZo6n heading--h5--3l5xQ3lN heading--white--2vAPsAl1 heading--noMargin--mnRHPAnD">
          <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/20/top-stories-thunderbolt-ipad-pro/">
           Top Stories: iPad Pro With Thunderbolt?, Intel Mocks M1 Macs, iMac Pro Officially Discontinued
          </a>
         </h2>
        </div>
        <div class="byline--3Eec5bcq">
         <time datetime="2021-03-20T06:00:17-07:00">
          Saturday March 20, 2021 6:00 am PDT
         </time>
         by
         <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/author/macrumors-staff/" rel="author">
          MacRumors Staff
         </a>
        </div>
        <div class="content--2u3grYDr js-content">
         <div class="ugc--2nTu61bm minor--3O_9dH4U" data-io-article-url="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/20/top-stories-thunderbolt-ipad-pro/">
          <div class="js-contentInner">
           <p>
            We're past the halfway point of March with no sign of an Apple media event, but that doesn't mean we won't be seeing an event or simply some product launches via press release in the coming weeks, as rumors of upcoming products continue to circulate.
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <div class="center-wrap">
            <div class="video-wrapper">
             <div class="video-container">
              <div class="ls_video_embed aspect-16-9 lazyload" data-thumb-size="maxresdefault" data-youtube="T8MLPk8UjFY" data-ytparams="modestbranding=1">
               <button class="play-btn">
                play
               </button>
              </div>
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="center-wrap">
            <em>
             <a href="//www.youtube.com/user/macrumors?sub_confirmation=1">
              Subscribe to the MacRumors YouTube channel
             </a>
             for more videos.
            </em>
           </div>
           <br/>
           Perhaps the biggest news topic this week was Justin Long of Apple's "Get a Mac" ad campaign from over a decade ago starring in a new campaign from Intel promoting Windows machines based on the company's processors as superior to Apple's new M1-based Macs. Check out our video above and read on below for details on these stories and more!
           <br/>
           <h3 class="h2-index">
            iPad Pro With Thunderbolt Port and Mini-LED Display Coming 'As Early As April'
           </h3>
           <p>
            <em>
             Bloomberg
            </em>
            's Mark Gurman this week reported that Apple plans to announce new iPads "as early as April," including new 11-inch and 12.9-inch iPad Pro models.
           </p>
           <p>
            <img alt="iPad Pro Mini LED yellow" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-768062 lazyload" data-sizes="auto" data-src="https://images.macrumors.com/t/z46pGTMtdUEpCr1FtIUt9Ipb8VM=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2020/11/iPad-Pro-Mini-LED-yellow.jpg?lossy" data-srcset="https://images.macrumors.com/t/z46pGTMtdUEpCr1FtIUt9Ipb8VM=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2020/11/iPad-Pro-Mini-LED-yellow.jpg?lossy 400w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/XYB5UC_H6AQZ0C75hnE-o5vnEtU=/800x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2020/11/iPad-Pro-Mini-LED-yellow.jpg?lossy 800w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/VkYi4qiwiOFBdYzV6v5hcgrPxNg=/1600x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2020/11/iPad-Pro-Mini-LED-yellow.jpg 1600w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/lY_phm92r9cuMakM8l01eKdfJyQ=/2500x0/filters:no_upscale():quality(90)/article-new/2020/11/iPad-Pro-Mini-LED-yellow.jpg 2500w" height="1080" src="https://images.macrumors.com/images-new/1x1.trans.gif" width="1920"/>
            <noscript>
             <img alt="iPad Pro Mini LED yellow" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-768062" height="1080" src="https://images.macrumors.com/article-new/2020/11/iPad-Pro-Mini-LED-yellow.jpg" width="1920"/>
            </noscript>
            <br/>
            Notably, Gurman claimed that
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/17/thunderbolt-ipad-pro-coming-in-april/">
             the new iPad Pro models could feature a Thunderbolt port
            </a>
            . This rumor certainly sounds plausible, as the new iPad Pro models are expected to be equipped with a faster A14X chip based on the M1 chip in the latest Macs, and the M1 chip supports Thunderbolt. And since Thunderbolt uses the USB-C connector design, the new iPad Pro models would still work with existing USB-C chargers and accessories.
           </p>
           <p>
            As widely rumored, Gurman said Apple is looking to include Mini-LED backlighting on the new 12.9-inch iPad Pro at a minimum, suggesting that the display technology might be exclusive to the larger model.
           </p>
           <p>
            Well-known Apple analyst Ming-Chi Kuo lent credence to this timeframe, claiming that
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/18/kuo-12-9-inch-mini-led-ipad-pro-production/">
             mass production of Mini-LED iPads will begin in mid-to-late April
            </a>
            . Kuo expects a
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/18/kuo-macbook-air-mini-led-2020-launch/">
             new MacBook Air with a Mini-LED display
            </a>
            and potentially a new iPad Air with an OLED display to follow in 2022.
            <br/>
           </p>
           <h3 class="h2-index">
            Apple Event in April? Recapping the Latest iPad Pro, AirPods, and AirTags Rumors
           </h3>
           <p>
            It's been a whirlwind of a month for Apple rumors. First, we heard from leaker Jon Prosser that an Apple Event was planned for March 16, but that was later ruled out by
            <em>
             Bloomberg
            </em>
            's Mark Gurman. Once that date passed, Prosser and other leakers then suggested there would be an Apple Event on March 23, which is seemingly not happening either.
           </p>
           <p>
            <img alt="aipad pro tags slight tweak feature" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-783347 lazyload" data-sizes="auto" data-src="https://images.macrumors.com/t/nKB8pzDreoIia6kUQvTOnEy_eD0=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/02/aipad-pro-tags-slight-tweak-feature.jpg?lossy" data-srcset="https://images.macrumors.com/t/nKB8pzDreoIia6kUQvTOnEy_eD0=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/02/aipad-pro-tags-slight-tweak-feature.jpg?lossy 400w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/haSa4G0Y34mvk5SWkEmjzNItRJQ=/800x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/02/aipad-pro-tags-slight-tweak-feature.jpg?lossy 800w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/4hBbKKia5PXdT_hyczFE8J8KkBM=/1600x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/02/aipad-pro-tags-slight-tweak-feature.jpg 1600w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/eWxG3uHfUqcrUbotBrosVi2yaEU=/2500x0/filters:no_upscale():quality(90)/article-new/2021/02/aipad-pro-tags-slight-tweak-feature.jpg 2500w" height="1080" src="https://images.macrumors.com/images-new/1x1.trans.gif" width="1920"/>
            <noscript>
             <img alt="aipad pro tags slight tweak feature" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-783347" height="1080" src="https://images.macrumors.com/article-new/2021/02/aipad-pro-tags-slight-tweak-feature.jpg" width="1920"/>
            </noscript>
            <br/>
            With attention now shifting to April for potential Apple announcements, we've put together
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/18/apple-event-april-rumor-recap/">
             a recap of the latest iPad Pro, AirPods, and AirTags rumors
            </a>
            from sources like Gurman and well-known analyst Ming-Chi Kuo.
           </p>
           <p>
            Beyond new iPad models, new products rumored to be in Apple's pipeline include its long-awaited AirTags item trackers, a new Apple TV with a stronger gaming focus, new AirPods and AirPods Pro, and more Apple silicon Macs, but some of these products are not expected until the second half of 2021.
            <br/>
           </p>
           <h3 class="h2-index">
            Former 'I'm a Mac' Actor Justin Long Throws Shade at M1 Macs in New Intel Ad Campaign
           </h3>
           <p>
            Justin Long, who starred in Apple's iconic "Get a Mac" ad campaign in the mid-2000s, has turned against the Mac in a new Intel ad campaign.
           </p>
           <p>
            <img alt="Justin Long Intel Feature Close" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-789383 lazyload" data-sizes="auto" data-src="https://images.macrumors.com/t/66EuQ03wSMOk6PORWCHpi3cBwWE=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/Justin-Long-Intel-Feature-Close.jpg?lossy" data-srcset="https://images.macrumors.com/t/66EuQ03wSMOk6PORWCHpi3cBwWE=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/Justin-Long-Intel-Feature-Close.jpg?lossy 400w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/V51KenqDUT9pz2GIMO2JiRqnLNE=/800x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/Justin-Long-Intel-Feature-Close.jpg?lossy 800w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/9KI1RfEdMs7yrallENxrYwHIlsY=/1600x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/Justin-Long-Intel-Feature-Close.jpg 1600w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/R6iBvOdGhO8amE60HkPpEpPgf28=/2500x0/filters:no_upscale():quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/Justin-Long-Intel-Feature-Close.jpg 2500w" height="1080" src="https://images.macrumors.com/images-new/1x1.trans.gif" width="1920"/>
            <noscript>
             <img alt="Justin Long Intel Feature Close" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-789383" height="1080" src="https://images.macrumors.com/article-new/2021/03/Justin-Long-Intel-Feature-Close.jpg" width="1920"/>
            </noscript>
            <br/>
            Intel's ad campaign
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/17/justin-long-get-a-mac-intel-ad-campaign/">
             attempts to poke holes at Apple's new M1 Macs
            </a>
            , including their official support for only a single external display (DisplayLink adapters
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2020/11/24/m1-macs-able-to-run-six-external-displays/">
             can be used as a workaround
            </a>
            ), support for a limited number of games, lack of a full-out touchscreen, and more.
           </p>
           <p>
            Intel's campaign has so far included a series of videos starring Long,
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/18/apple-launches-pc-vs-mac-comparison-website/">
             a website comparing the M1 chip to Intel processors
            </a>
            , and social media content, including a photo of
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/18/intel-anti-dongle-m1-mac-ad/">
             Long holding several dongles in his hand
            </a>
            .
           </p>
           <p>
            The first M1 Macs have received rave reviews, with the M1 MacBook Air outperforming a maxed-out 16-inch MacBook Pro with Intel's Core i9 processor in Geekbench benchmark scores.
            <br/>
           </p>
           <h3 class="h2-index">
            iMac Pro Officially Discontinued, Removed From Apple's Site and No Longer Available for Purchase
           </h3>
           <p>
            Two weeks after Apple announced that it was discontinuing the iMac Pro and noted that orders would only be available while supplies lasted, it appears the high-end all-in-one desktop
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/19/imac-pro-officially-discontinued/">
             has reached the end of the line
            </a>
            . Apple this week stopped taking orders for the machine and removed it from the Mac section of the company's website.
           </p>
           <p>
            <img alt="iMac Pro Alert Feature" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-787647 lazyload" data-sizes="auto" data-src="https://images.macrumors.com/t/fhna1R9kcHaX6KtiD3OiEjtirtQ=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/iMac-Pro-Alert-Feature.jpg?lossy" data-srcset="https://images.macrumors.com/t/fhna1R9kcHaX6KtiD3OiEjtirtQ=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/iMac-Pro-Alert-Feature.jpg?lossy 400w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/KvHSGt-lw4bLcqVEU5vzw4c_cTQ=/800x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/iMac-Pro-Alert-Feature.jpg?lossy 800w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/-SQtPEgIN_YEYe5lgOk92xKZyJs=/1600x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/iMac-Pro-Alert-Feature.jpg 1600w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/-vdaX1OKIJBx88ZNvzx6hILus0w=/2500x0/filters:no_upscale():quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/iMac-Pro-Alert-Feature.jpg 2500w" height="1268" src="https://images.macrumors.com/images-new/1x1.trans.gif" width="2254"/>
            <noscript>
             <img alt="iMac Pro Alert Feature" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-787647" height="1268" src="https://images.macrumors.com/article-new/2021/03/iMac-Pro-Alert-Feature.jpg" width="2254"/>
            </noscript>
            <br/>
            Apple recommends that users who are looking for a high-end Mac choose the 27-inch iMac, which was last refreshed in August 2020. The current 27-inch iMac configured with a 10-core Core i9 processor is faster and more affordable than the standard iMac Pro with a 10-core Xeon W processor was. Apple is also expected to introduce a redesigned iMac based on Apple silicon chips later this year.
            <br/>
           </p>
           <h3 class="h2-index">
            Hands-On: Kensington's New $400 StudioDock for iPad Pro
           </h3>
           <p>
            Kensington in February began accepting pre-orders for the StudioDock docking station that it released for the iPad Pro, and now those StudioDock orders have started arriving to customers. We picked up one of the new StudioDocks to see if it's worth the high purchase price for an iPad workflow.
           </p>
           <p>
            <img alt="400 iPad Dock Feature tighter" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-789220 lazyload" data-sizes="auto" data-src="https://images.macrumors.com/t/CLQkrQJD04X7zE2HPQZrdzFSzSg=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/400-iPad-Dock-Feature-tighter.jpg?lossy" data-srcset="https://images.macrumors.com/t/CLQkrQJD04X7zE2HPQZrdzFSzSg=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/400-iPad-Dock-Feature-tighter.jpg?lossy 400w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/1FZQVuBHwVQFBO5tdwscAHfijH8=/800x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/400-iPad-Dock-Feature-tighter.jpg?lossy 800w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/-24GkiBSCZ5mo5YRQZSmqsAcsDY=/1600x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/400-iPad-Dock-Feature-tighter.jpg 1600w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/Vdd6jGyZgWyd5X-oZ1luMufWv6I=/2500x0/filters:no_upscale():quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/400-iPad-Dock-Feature-tighter.jpg 2500w" height="1341" src="https://images.macrumors.com/images-new/1x1.trans.gif" width="2456"/>
            <noscript>
             <img alt="400 iPad Dock Feature tighter" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-789220" height="1341" src="https://images.macrumors.com/article-new/2021/03/400-iPad-Dock-Feature-tighter.jpg" width="2456"/>
            </noscript>
            <br/>
            Available for the 11-inch iPad Pro, 12.9-inch iPad Pro, and 10.9-inch iPad Air, the StudioDock has a magnetic base where an iPad can attach, and it can be used in either landscape or portrait mode. We have the version for the 12.9-inch iPad Pro, and it resembles Apple's Pro Display XDR stand.
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/16/kensington-studiodock-ipad-pro/">
             Watch our hands-on video for our complete impressions.
            </a>
            <br/>
           </p>
           <h3 class="h2-index">
            iPhone 13 Models Will 'Likely' Have 'Touch ID' Under the Display
           </h3>
           <p>
            iPhone 13 models slated for release later this year
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/12/iphone-13-touch-id-under-display/">
             will "likely" feature a fingerprint scanner embedded under the display
            </a>
            for authentication, in addition to Face ID, according to Barclays Research analyst Andrew Gardiner and three of his colleagues.
           </p>
           <p>
            <img alt="under display touch id" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-789903 lazyload" data-sizes="auto" data-src="https://images.macrumors.com/t/XEWFmhG7c0kfsKyybfO0EpErrvo=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/under-display-touch-id.jpg?lossy" data-srcset="https://images.macrumors.com/t/XEWFmhG7c0kfsKyybfO0EpErrvo=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/under-display-touch-id.jpg?lossy 400w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/Tx4ANFYCkGzPsSe9vtU6ZuyBLBQ=/800x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/under-display-touch-id.jpg?lossy 800w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/c-XfQp7NsF3CpcAMGCTe-VmgC8w=/1600x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/under-display-touch-id.jpg 1600w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/Wba5ko3ujASQCY6IRTTQrrlDLPc=/2500x0/filters:no_upscale():quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/under-display-touch-id.jpg 2500w" height="1080" src="https://images.macrumors.com/images-new/1x1.trans.gif" width="1920"/>
            <noscript>
             <img alt="under display touch id" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-789903" height="1080" src="https://images.macrumors.com/article-new/2021/03/under-display-touch-id.jpg" width="1920"/>
            </noscript>
            <br/>
            Under-display "Touch ID" for iPhones has been rumored several times over the last few years. Bloomberg's Mark Gurman and The Wall Street Journal's Joanna Stern have also claimed that Apple is at least testing an under-display fingerprint scanner for iPhone 13 models, so time will tell whether the feature makes the cut.
           </p>
           <p>
            Apple has filed various
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/18/apple-enhanced-under-display-touch-id-system/amp/">
             under-display fingerprint scanner patents
            </a>
            as part of its research and development of the feature.
            <br/>
           </p>

       <article class="article--2pJwZBkO js-article front--3uTQDaAu f_front" expanded="false">
        <div class="titlebar--3N4MCKxL">
         <h2 class="heading--1cooZo6n heading--h5--3l5xQ3lN heading--white--2vAPsAl1 heading--noMargin--mnRHPAnD">
          <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/20/apple-must-pay-308-million-infringed-drm-patent/">
           Apple Ordered to Pay $309 Million for Infringing DRM Patent
          </a>
         </h2>
        </div>
        <div class="byline--3Eec5bcq">
         <time datetime="2021-03-20T03:01:58-07:00">
          Saturday March 20, 2021 3:01 am PDT
         </time>
         by
         <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/author/tim-hardwick/" rel="author">
          Tim Hardwick
         </a>
        </div>
        <div class="content--2u3grYDr js-content">
         <div class="ugc--2nTu61bm minor--3O_9dH4U" data-io-article-url="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/20/apple-must-pay-308-million-infringed-drm-patent/">
          <div class="js-contentInner">
           <p>
            A federal jury in Texas has ordered Apple to pay around $308.5 million to a local licensing firm for infringing a patent related to digital rights management, reports
            <em>
             <a href="https://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2021-03-19/apple-told-to-pay-308-5-million-for-infringing-drm-patent">
              Bloomberg
             </a>
            </em>
            .
           </p>
           <p>
            <img alt="PMClogonewer" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-789954 lazyload" data-sizes="auto" data-src="https://images.macrumors.com/t/vvAFH0QEfElfHMJ90N96ARdadWw=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/PMClogonewer.jpg?lossy" data-srcset="https://images.macrumors.com/t/vvAFH0QEfElfHMJ90N96ARdadWw=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/PMClogonewer.jpg?lossy 400w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/fIMshar1h8eJ-Bqp5ZdaGzlsqnE=/800x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/PMClogonewer.jpg?lossy 800w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/2qq_sq1TkJHnmHIYakeDi3H8Op8=/1600x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/PMClogonewer.jpg 1600w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/SuY1jHyP_cq6b8TprLGum3lDw5I=/2500x0/filters:no_upscale():quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/PMClogonewer.jpg 2500w" height="627" src="https://images.macrumors.com/images-new/1x1.trans.gif" width="1200"/>
            <noscript>
             <img alt="PMClogonewer" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-789954" height="627" src="https://images.macrumors.com/article-new/2021/03/PMClogonewer.jpg" width="1200"/>
            </noscript>
            <br/>
            Following a five-day trial, jurors on Friday said Apple must pay running loyalty fees to Texas-based
            <a href="https://www.personalizedmedia.com">
             Personalized Media Communications
            </a>
            (PMC). A running loyalty is generally based on the amount of sales of a product or service.
           </p>
           <p>
            PMC originally sued Apple in 2015 for allegedly infringing seven of its patents. As part of the legal action, the company claimed Apple infringed its patent with technology including FairPlay, which is used to distribute encrypted content through the company's iTunes,
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/guide/app-store/">
             App Store
            </a>
            , and
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/guide/apple-music/">
             Apple Music
            </a>
            apps.
           </p>
           <p>
            Apple successfully challenged PMC's case at the U.S. patent office, but an appeals court reversed that decision in March 2020, opening an avenue for a trial to proceed.
           </p>
           <p>
            Apple told
            <em>
             Bloomberg
            </em>
            it was disappointed with Friday's ruling and would appeal the decision.
            <br/>
           </p>
           <blockquote>
            <p>
             "Cases like this, brought by companies that don't make or sell any products, stifle innovation and ultimately harm consumers," the company said in an emailed statement.
            </p>
           </blockquote>
           <p>
            PMC is a non-practicing entity that holds a patent portfolio and generates revenue through patent litigation. When such companies employ hardball legal tactics to enforce patent rights far beyond the patent's actual value, they are often referred to as patent trolls.
           </p>
           <p>
            The Sugarland-based company has infringement cases pending against several other tech companies including Netflix, Google, and Amazon.
           </p>
           <div class="linkback">
            Tags:
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/guide/lawsuit/">
             lawsuit
            </a>
            ,
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/guide/patent-trials/">
             patent trials
            </a>
            ,
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/guide/patent-lawsuits/">
             Patent lawsuits
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>

            Show Full Article
           </a>
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>

       <article class="article--2pJwZBkO js-article front--3uTQDaAu f_front f_apple-tv-shows" expanded="false">
        <div class="titlebar--3N4MCKxL">
         <h2 class="heading--1cooZo6n heading--h5--3l5xQ3lN heading--white--2vAPsAl1 heading--noMargin--mnRHPAnD">
          <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/20/apple-restaurant-partnership-servant-season-2/">
           Apple Partners With Restaurants to Offer Free Pizza in Celebration of 'Servant' Season 2 Finale
          </a>
         </h2>
        </div>
        <div class="byline--3Eec5bcq">
         <time datetime="2021-03-19T22:07:23-07:00">
          Friday March 19, 2021 10:07 pm PDT
         </time>
         by
         <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/author/frank-mcshan/" rel="author">
          Frank McShan
         </a>
        </div>
        <div class="content--2u3grYDr js-content">
         <div class="ugc--2nTu61bm minor--3O_9dH4U" data-io-article-url="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/20/apple-restaurant-partnership-servant-season-2/">
          <div class="js-contentInner">
           <p>
            Apple is partnering with two Los Angeles-based restaurants this weekend to offer free pizza in celebration of the second-season finale of the
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/guide/apple-tv-plus/">
             Apple TV+
            </a>
            show "Servant." The promotion pays homage to "Cheezus Crust," a fictional pizza delivery business in the show.
           </p>
           <p>
            <img alt="Servant Apple TV Plus Pizza" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-789932 lazyload" data-sizes="auto" data-src="https://images.macrumors.com/t/uuPV5D37cbzaZ_ljx9cSwpWRMKI=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/Servant-Apple-TV-Plus-Pizza.jpg?lossy" data-srcset="https://images.macrumors.com/t/uuPV5D37cbzaZ_ljx9cSwpWRMKI=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/Servant-Apple-TV-Plus-Pizza.jpg?lossy 400w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/ErUquJdOHxupEexUvCchHfJ76gA=/800x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/Servant-Apple-TV-Plus-Pizza.jpg?lossy 800w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/N6gxeu6fMW6wCo0ia3F7mNixRZ4=/1600x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/Servant-Apple-TV-Plus-Pizza.jpg 1600w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/iH45bXI1pkx83j0caJJXSmksd_s=/2500x0/filters:no_upscale():quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/Servant-Apple-TV-Plus-Pizza.jpg 2500w" height="1080" src="https://images.macrumors.com/images-new/1x1.trans.gif" width="1920"/>
            <noscript>
             <img alt="Servant Apple TV Plus Pizza" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-789932" height="1080" src="https://images.macrumors.com/article-new/2021/03/Servant-Apple-TV-Plus-Pizza.jpg" width="1920"/>
            </noscript>
            <br/>
            Those in Los Angeles can order the free pizza from either
            <a href="https://www.grubhub.com/restaurant/gjelina-take-away-1427-abbot-kinney-blvd-venice/2331716">
             Gjelina
            </a>
            or
            <a href="https://www.grubhub.com/restaurant/milo--olive-2723-wilshire-blvd-santa-monica/439571">
             Milo &amp; Olive
            </a>
            through Grubhub, with the offer lasting through Sunday or until supplies last. The pizza's toppings include duck sausage, confit leeks, shimeiji mushroom, nameko mushrooms, mozzarella, and thyme, echoing the use of occasionally peculiar food in "Servant." The pizza is listed at $30, but the discount will be applied at checkout.
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <div class="center-wrap">
            <blockquote class="twitter-tweet">
             <p dir="ltr" lang="en">
              The Turners launch Cheezus Crust, a pizza delivery service, in Season 2 of
              <a href="https://twitter.com/Servant?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw">
               @Servant
              </a>
              . To celebrate the finale, were bringing free pizza to LA exclusively on
              <a href="https://twitter.com/Grubhub?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw">
               @grubhub
              </a>
              this weekend. Starting today at 5PM PST.
              <a href="https://twitter.com/Gjelina?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw">
               @Gjelina
              </a>
              :
              <a href="https://t.co/7T43XbSOXQ">
               https://t.co/7T43XbSOXQ
              </a>
              <a href="https://twitter.com/MiloandOlive?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw">
               @MiloandOlive
              </a>
              :
              <a href="https://t.co/jhiwr3BGgt">
               https://t.co/jhiwr3BGgt
              </a>
              <a href="https://t.co/A5uqSqtjrn">
               pic.twitter.com/A5uqSqtjrn
              </a>
              
              <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/roundup/apple-tv/">
               Apple TV
              </a>
              (@AppleTV)
              <a href="https://twitter.com/AppleTV/status/1373048939797041155?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw">
               March 19, 2021
              </a>
             </p>
            </blockquote>
            <script async="" charset="utf-8" src="//platform.twitter.com/widgets.js">
            </script>
           </div>
           <br/>
           "Servant," a horror thriller produced by M. Night Shyamalan, follows a Philadelphia couple who are in mourning after losing their child. Their baby, Jericho, is replaced by a reborn doll that Dorothy, the mother, thinks is real, and a strange nanny, Leanne, is hired to look after the doll. After Leanne's arrival, bizarre things begin happening to the family.
           <p>
            "Servant" was one of the first series on Apple TV+, and it was popular with Apple TV+ subscribers. Apple
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2020/12/15/servant-apple-tv-plus-series-3/">
             renewed the show for a third season
            </a>
            in December.
           </p>
           <div class="linkback">
            Tags:
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/guide/apple-tv-shows/">
             Apple TV Shows
            </a>
            ,
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/guide/apple-tv-plus/">
             Apple TV Plus Guide
            </a>
           </div>

       <article class="article--2pJwZBkO js-article front--3uTQDaAu f_front" expanded="false">
        <div class="titlebar--3N4MCKxL">
         <h2 class="heading--1cooZo6n heading--h5--3l5xQ3lN heading--white--2vAPsAl1 heading--noMargin--mnRHPAnD">
          <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/20/apple-vs-epic-trial-tim-cook-scott-forstall/">
           Tim Cook, Craig Federighi, Phil Schiller and Scott Forstall to Testify in Epic v. Apple Trial
          </a>
         </h2>
        </div>
        <div class="byline--3Eec5bcq">
         <time datetime="2021-03-19T21:49:32-07:00">
          Friday March 19, 2021 9:49 pm PDT
         </time>
         by
         <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/author/juli-clover/" rel="author">
          Juli Clover
         </a>
        </div>
        <div class="content--2u3grYDr js-content">
         <div class="ugc--2nTu61bm minor--3O_9dH4U" data-io-article-url="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/20/apple-vs-epic-trial-tim-cook-scott-forstall/">
          <div class="js-contentInner">
           <p>
            Apple today submitted its witness list for its upcoming bench trial with
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/guide/epic-games/">
             Epic Games
            </a>
            , and several Apple executives will be testifying, including Apple CEO
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/guide/tim-cook/">
             Tim Cook
            </a>
            , Apple Fellow
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/guide/phil-schiller/">
             Phil Schiller
            </a>
            , and Apple Senior Vice President of Software Engineering Craig Federighi.
           </p>
           <p>
            <img alt="fortnite apple logo 2" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-756080 lazyload" data-sizes="auto" data-src="https://images.macrumors.com/t/zTsPhtXDA93pBczH7gQJEDFbmfk=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2020/08/fortnite-apple-logo-2.5.jpg?lossy" data-srcset="https://images.macrumors.com/t/zTsPhtXDA93pBczH7gQJEDFbmfk=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2020/08/fortnite-apple-logo-2.5.jpg?lossy 400w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/sagVUf05yYVThpdJVMlGMAdxZ9w=/800x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2020/08/fortnite-apple-logo-2.5.jpg?lossy 800w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/0L2v9XjttdSoyaE8uTeKN-cSaBY=/1600x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2020/08/fortnite-apple-logo-2.5.jpg 1600w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/xk0KQv06cFOtW0fqN5_440jLWRM=/2500x0/filters:no_upscale():quality(90)/article-new/2020/08/fortnite-apple-logo-2.5.jpg 2500w" height="720" src="https://images.macrumors.com/images-new/1x1.trans.gif" width="1280"/>
            <noscript>
             <img alt="fortnite apple logo 2" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-756080" height="720" src="https://images.macrumors.com/article-new/2020/08/fortnite-apple-logo-2.5.jpg" width="1280"/>
            </noscript>
            <br/>
            Cook will be directly examined for one hour, with a one hour cross examination also included. Federighi will testify for two hours with a one hour cross examination, while Schiller, who is in charge of the
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/guide/app-store/">
             App Store
            </a>
            , will testify for a total of 10 hours. All of Apple's witnesses will appear in person.
           </p>
           <p>
            In a statement to
            <em>
             MacRumors
            </em>
            , Apple said that its executives are eager to share the impact the App Store has had on innovation and economies around the world.
           </p>
           <blockquote>
            <p>
             Our senior executives look forward to sharing with the court the very positive impact the App Store has had on innovation, economies across the world and the customer experience over the last 12 years. We feel confident the case will prove that Epic purposefully breached its agreement solely to increase its revenues, which is what resulted in their removal from the App Store. By doing that, Epic circumvented the security features of the App Store in a way that would lead to reduced competition and put consumers' privacy and data security at tremendous risk.
            </p>
           </blockquote>
           <p>
            Apple's witness list also includes App Store Vice President Matt Fischer, Head of Fraud Engineering Algorithms and Risk Eric Friedman, Director of Commerce and Payments Eric Gray, Game Development Manager Mark Grimm, and other employees in marketing, developer relations, and related fields.
           </p>
           <p>
            Epic's witnesses include Epic Games CEO Tim Sweeney and other Epic employees, and third-party witnesses will include executives from Facebook, Microsoft, Nvidia, plus iTunes chief
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/guide/eddy-cue/">
             Eddy Cue
            </a>
            and former iOS software chief Scott Forstall. Epic said in February that it was attempting to get in touch with Forstall, but was
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/02/23/epic-games-scott-forstall-apple-legal-battle/">
             having difficulty
            </a>
            locating him. Epic plans to call on Forstall because of his involvement with the launch of the App Store prior to his 2013 departure from the company. In a statement, Epic said that it is not alone in its fight with Apple.
           </p>
           <blockquote>
            <p>
             The chorus of developers speaking out against Apple and their anticompetitive practices has become louder. We are not alone in this fight. We look forward to making our case for competition in app distribution and payment processes.
            </p>
           </blockquote>
           <p>
            The trial is
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/01/epic-vs-apple-in-person-trial-may-3/">
             set to begin
            </a>
            on Monday, May 3. It is a bench trial, which means there will be no jury involved. Earlier this month, Judge Yvonne Gonzalez pushed for an in-person trial as she said that the case is "significant enough" that the court should hear it in person.
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <div class="center-wrap">
            <div class="scribd-maxwidth">
             <iframe class="scribd_iframe_embed" data-aspect-ratio="0.7729220222793488" data-auto-height="true" frameborder="0" height="600" scrolling="no" src="https://www.scribd.com/embeds/499519972/content?start_page=1&amp;view_mode=scroll&amp;access_key=key-Eo3QpyVDA9YlnPuJkjae" tabindex="0" title="Apple's Tentative Initial Witness List for Epic v. Apple" width="100%">
             </iframe>
            </div>
            <p style="   margin: 12px auto 6px auto;   font-family: Helvetica,Arial,Sans-serif;   font-style: normal;   font-variant: normal;   font-weight: normal;   font-size: 14px;   line-height: normal;   font-size-adjust: none;   font-stretch: normal;   -x-system-font: none;   display: block;">
             <a href="https://www.scribd.com/document/499519972/Apple-s-Tentative-Initial-Witness-List-for-Epic-v-Apple#from_embed" style="text-decoration: underline;" title="View Apple's Tentative Initial Witness List for Epic v. Apple on Scribd">
              Apple's Tentative Initi...
             </a>
             by
             <a href="https://www.scribd.com/user/212523051/MacRumors#from_embed" style="text-decoration: underline;" title="View MacRumors's profile on Scribd">
              MacRumors
             </a>
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="linkback">
            Tags:
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/guide/tim-cook/">

            </a>

             Phil Schiller
            </a>
            ,
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/guide/scott-forstall/">
             Scott Forstall
            </a>
            ,
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/guide/craig-federighi/">

            </a>

       <article class="article--2pJwZBkO js-article front--3uTQDaAu f_front" expanded="false">
        <div class="titlebar--3N4MCKxL">
         <h2 class="heading--1cooZo6n heading--h5--3l5xQ3lN heading--white--2vAPsAl1 heading--noMargin--mnRHPAnD">
          <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/19/imac-pro-officially-discontinued/">
           iMac Pro Officially Discontinued, Removed From Apple's Site and No Longer Available for Purchase
          </a>
         </h2>
        </div>
        <div class="byline--3Eec5bcq">
         <time datetime="2021-03-19T13:24:49-07:00">
          Friday March 19, 2021 1:24 pm PDT
         </time>
         by
         <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/author/juli-clover/" rel="author">
          Juli Clover
         </a>
        </div>
        <div class="content--2u3grYDr js-content">
         <div class="ugc--2nTu61bm minor--3O_9dH4U" data-io-article-url="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/19/imac-pro-officially-discontinued/">
          <div class="js-contentInner">
           <p>
            The
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/roundup/imac-pro/">
             iMac Pro
            </a>
            has been officially discontinued as of this afternoon, with the machine no longer available for purchase from the online Apple Store.
           </p>
           <p>
            <img alt="imac pro after effects" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-609653 lazyload" data-sizes="auto" data-src="https://images.macrumors.com/t/5Y0XJOm19jOE1OQQZY0ECuKTmsI=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2017/12/imac-pro-after-effects.jpg?lossy" data-srcset="https://images.macrumors.com/t/5Y0XJOm19jOE1OQQZY0ECuKTmsI=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2017/12/imac-pro-after-effects.jpg?lossy 400w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/5B65g9Hn_Vrj2nDOdvS31XWyfw4=/800x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2017/12/imac-pro-after-effects.jpg?lossy 800w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/lVUg8g5xxWwlEnKTCHar4L1g2Nc=/1600x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2017/12/imac-pro-after-effects.jpg 1600w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/2YQ1nSlP0JkYOY1bGW-IQlJQN48=/2500x0/filters:no_upscale():quality(90)/article-new/2017/12/imac-pro-after-effects.jpg 2500w" height="660" src="https://images.macrumors.com/images-new/1x1.trans.gif" width="800"/>
            <noscript>
             <img alt="imac pro after effects" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-609653" height="660" src="https://images.macrumors.com/article-new/2017/12/imac-pro-after-effects.jpg" width="800"/>
            </noscript>
            <br/>
            The iMac Pro
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/19/imac-pro-currently-unavailable-in-us/">
             went out of stock
            </a>
            in the United States and other countries earlier today, and now, the iMac Pro page has been removed entirely from Apple's website.
           </p>
           <p>
            With the iMac Pro page eliminated, there is no longer an option to buy an iMac Pro in the United States or in any other country, and the machine is no longer listed in the Apple Store app, nor does a search bring up iMac Pro listings.
           </p>
           <p>
            Apple has also changed the
            <a href="https://www.apple.com/shop/accessories/all/whats-new?page=1&amp;f=27imacpro_2017&amp;fh=47a9%2B499c">
             Mac compatibility filter
            </a>
            for the iMac Pro to say "2017" instead of "2017 and later," making it clear that there will be no more iMac Pro models in the future.
           </p>
           <p>
            Apple first announced plans
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/06/apple-confirms-imac-pro-will-be-discontinued/">
             to discontinue
            </a>
            the iMac Pro in early March, and said at the time that the iMac Pro
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/06/imac-pro-while-supplies-last/">
             would be available
            </a>
            for purchase "while supplies last," but supplies have apparently dried up.
           </p>
           <p>
            Though Apple has removed the iMac Pro from its website following its discontinuation, there are still a variety of iMac Pro models available from
            <a href="https://www.apple.com/shop/refurbished/mac/imac-pro">
             Apple's refurbished store
            </a>
            .
           </p>
           <p>
            Apple recommends that users who are looking for a high-end Mac choose the 27-inch
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/roundup/imac/">
             iMac
            </a>
            , which was last refreshed in August 2020. The current 27-inch iMac configured with a 10-core Core i9 processor is faster and more affordable than the standard iMac Pro with a 10-core Xeon W processor was.
           </p>
           <p>
            Apple is also working on
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/01/15/apple-redesigned-imacs-slimmer-bezels/">
             a redesigned iMac
            </a>
            that will feature slimmer bezels, a Pro Display XDR-style design, and Apple silicon chips, so those who are seeking a powerful desktop machine may want to wait until the new iMac models come out later this year before making a purchase.
           </p>
          </div>
          <div class="desktopExpandWrap--197SeUpp js-expandWrap">
           <a class="button button--2VOdSzvH js-teaseTrigger" href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/19/imac-pro-officially-discontinued/">
            Show Full Article
           </a>
          </div>
         </div>

       <article class="article--2pJwZBkO js-article front--3uTQDaAu f_front" expanded="false">
        <div class="titlebar--3N4MCKxL">
         <h2 class="heading--1cooZo6n heading--h5--3l5xQ3lN heading--white--2vAPsAl1 heading--noMargin--mnRHPAnD">
          <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/19/apple-stops-signing-ios-14-4-1/">
           Apple Stops Signing iOS 14.4 Following Release of iOS 14.4.1
          </a>
         </h2>
        </div>
        <div class="byline--3Eec5bcq">
         <time datetime="2021-03-19T13:23:16-07:00">
          Friday March 19, 2021 1:23 pm PDT
         </time>
         by
         <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/author/juli-clover/" rel="author">
          Juli Clover
         </a>
        </div>
        <div class="content--2u3grYDr js-content">
         <div class="ugc--2nTu61bm minor--3O_9dH4U" data-io-article-url="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/19/apple-stops-signing-ios-14-4-1/">
          <div class="js-contentInner">
           <p>
            Following the
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/08/apple-releases-ios-14-4-1/">
             release of iOS 14.4.1
            </a>
            on March 8, Apple has stopped signing iOS 14.4, the previous version of
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/roundup/ios-14/">
             iOS 14
            </a>
            . With the software no longer being signed, it is no longer possible to downgrade from iOS 14.4.1 to iOS 14.4 if you've already upgraded your
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/guide/iphone/">
             iPhone
            </a>
            or
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/roundup/ipad/">
             iPad
            </a>
            .
           </p>
           <p>
            <img alt="iOS 14" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-787618 lazyload" data-sizes="auto" data-src="https://images.macrumors.com/t/dTTJRONbeP5g1xOo_SXBsXVN-aE=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/iOS-14.4.1-on-phone.jpg?lossy" data-srcset="https://images.macrumors.com/t/dTTJRONbeP5g1xOo_SXBsXVN-aE=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/iOS-14.4.1-on-phone.jpg?lossy 400w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/3y8sxLfWAO-1Q84u6Wz3KPkJiWo=/800x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/iOS-14.4.1-on-phone.jpg?lossy 800w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/f3SY_lkTyuufv9zYo1AMTzAEJvk=/1600x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/iOS-14.4.1-on-phone.jpg 1600w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/Q9x1JdLSg_zZiCZThM-x-Rw39_8=/2500x0/filters:no_upscale():quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/iOS-14.4.1-on-phone.jpg 2500w" height="1406" src="https://images.macrumors.com/images-new/1x1.trans.gif" width="2500"/>
            <noscript>
             <img alt="iOS 14" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-787618" height="1406" src="https://images.macrumors.com/article-new/2021/03/iOS-14.4.1-on-phone.jpg" width="2500"/>
            </noscript>
            <br/>
            Apple routinely stops signing older versions of software updates after new releases come out in order to encourage customers to keep their operating systems up to date.
           </p>
           <p>
            iOS 14.4.1 was a
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/08/apple-releases-ios-14-4-1/">
             security fix update
            </a>
            that addressed a WebKit vulnerability that could allow maliciously crafted web content to execute code.
           </p>
           <p>
            iOS 14.4.1 is the current publicly available version of iOS that people can download, but Apple has also
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/guide/everything-new-in-ios-14-5-beta/">
             provided iOS 14.5
            </a>
            to developers and public beta testers for testing purposes. iOS 14.5 is one of the biggest updates to iOS 14 to date, introducing a feature for unlocking an iPhone when wearing a mask with an Apple Watch, adding Dual-SIM 5G support, introducing compatibility with the latest gaming controllers, and more.
           </p>
          </div>
          <div class="desktopExpandWrap--197SeUpp js-expandWrap">
           <a class="button button--2VOdSzvH js-teaseTrigger" href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/19/apple-stops-signing-ios-14-4-1/">
            Show Full Article
           </a>
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>

        <div class="titlebar--3N4MCKxL">
         <h2 class="heading--1cooZo6n heading--h5--3l5xQ3lN heading--white--2vAPsAl1 heading--noMargin--mnRHPAnD">
          <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/19/faze-clan-powerbeats-pro/">
           Apple Teams Up With FaZe Clan for Exclusive Powerbeats Pro
          </a>
         </h2>
        </div>
        <div class="byline--3Eec5bcq">
         <time datetime="2021-03-19T13:06:42-07:00">
          Friday March 19, 2021 1:06 pm PDT
         </time>
         by
         <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/author/juli-clover/" rel="author">
          Juli Clover
         </a>
        </div>
        <div class="content--2u3grYDr js-content">
         <div class="ugc--2nTu61bm minor--3O_9dH4U" data-io-article-url="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/19/faze-clan-powerbeats-pro/">
          <div class="js-contentInner">
           <p>
            Apple's Beats by Dre brand today announced
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/guide/powerbeats-pro/">
             Powerbeats Pro
            </a>
            in a new colorway that's being released as part of a collaboration with FaZe Clan.
           </p>
           <p>
            <img alt="faze powerbeats pro" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-789885 lazyload" data-sizes="auto" data-src="https://images.macrumors.com/t/pP1REUVoF9LiDDqxnb76pYKTiww=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/faze-powerbeats-pro.jpg?lossy" data-srcset="https://images.macrumors.com/t/pP1REUVoF9LiDDqxnb76pYKTiww=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/faze-powerbeats-pro.jpg?lossy 400w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/kAN0a7VFpZxt3ZXirlTfoxt2vOM=/800x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/faze-powerbeats-pro.jpg?lossy 800w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/Fvp0Hh1-njPasYvjdZa4otS_cOI=/1600x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/faze-powerbeats-pro.jpg 1600w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/zSr5t1VRI6HIAkmUyuWj3DtBQyM=/2500x0/filters:no_upscale():quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/faze-powerbeats-pro.jpg 2500w" height="608" src="https://images.macrumors.com/images-new/1x1.trans.gif" width="1080"/>
            <noscript>
             <img alt="faze powerbeats pro" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-789885" height="608" src="https://images.macrumors.com/article-new/2021/03/faze-powerbeats-pro.jpg" width="1080"/>
            </noscript>
            <br/>
            <a href="https://fazeclan.com">
             FaZe Clan
            </a>
            is a professional esports organization and its merchandise is largely red and black, so Apple has designed red and black Powerbeats Pro in the pattern that FaZe Clan often uses.
           </p>
           <p>
            According
            <a href="https://twitter.com/beatsbydre/status/1372979648276086786">
             to a tweet
            </a>
            from the Beats by Dre Twitter account, the FaZe Clan Powerbeats Pro will be limited edition and will be
            <a href="https://apps.apple.com/us/app/the-ntwrk/id1425910407?_branch_match_id=758349708828931192">
             sold through NTWRK
            </a>
            , an app that allows customers to shop limited edition sneaker and streetwear drops. The FaZe Clan Powerbeats Pro will be available on March 22.
           </p>
           <p>
            Apple
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2020/05/29/powerbeats-pro-new-colors/">
             previously teamed up
            </a>
            with FaZe Clan for the launch of the Powerbeats Pro in spring colors in May 2020. Beats by Dre used a drone to send the Powerbeats Pro to members of the FaZe Clan.
           </p>

       <article class="article--2pJwZBkO js-article front--3uTQDaAu f_front" expanded="false">
        <div class="titlebar--3N4MCKxL">
         <h2 class="heading--1cooZo6n heading--h5--3l5xQ3lN heading--white--2vAPsAl1 heading--noMargin--mnRHPAnD">
          <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/19/handy-iphone-shortcuts/">
           Handy iPhone and iPad Shortcuts You Should Check Out
          </a>
         </h2>
        </div>
        <div class="byline--3Eec5bcq">
         <time datetime="2021-03-19T12:31:34-07:00">
          Friday March 19, 2021 12:31 pm PDT
         </time>
         by
         <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/author/juli-clover/" rel="author">
          Juli Clover
         </a>
        </div>
        <div class="content--2u3grYDr js-content">
         <div class="ugc--2nTu61bm minor--3O_9dH4U" data-io-article-url="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/19/handy-iphone-shortcuts/">
          <div class="js-contentInner">
           <p>
            With the launch of iOS 13, Apple introduced Shortcuts support and the Shortcuts app, adding a whole range of new functionality to the iPhone. Shortcuts have continued to be popular since their debut, and in iOS 14, the addition of Home screen widgets made it even easier to get to your Shortcuts, so we thought we'd round up some of our most useful Shortcut options for iPhone and iPad.
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <div class="center-wrap">
            <div class="video-wrapper">
             <div class="video-container">
              <div class="ls_video_embed aspect-16-9 lazyload" data-thumb-size="maxresdefault" data-youtube="eU1rW9To0s4" data-ytparams="modestbranding=1">
               <button class="play-btn">
                play
               </button>
              </div>
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="center-wrap">
            <em>
             <a href="//www.youtube.com/user/macrumors?sub_confirmation=1">
              Subscribe to the MacRumors YouTube channel
             </a>
             for more videos.
            </em>
           </div>
           <ul>
            <li>
             <a href="https://routinehub.co/shortcut/7620/">
              <strong>
               Photos Toolkit
              </strong>
             </a>
             - Photos ToolKit is an all-in-one shortcut that can resize images, convert images to different formats, rotate images, combine images in a collage, make GIFs, and more.
            </li>
            <li>
             <a href="https://www.icloud.com/shortcuts/534bc73670064501895f5982c07a2d13">
              <strong>
               Make PDF
              </strong>
             </a>
             - As the name suggests, the Make PDF shortcut can turn documents and webpages into PDFs.
            </li>
            <li>
             <a href="https://www.macstories.net/ios/shortcuts-corner-apple-frames-for-iphone-12-and-se-get-image-resolution-encode-images-to-base64-and-search-articles-in-reeder/">
              <strong>
               Apple Frames
              </strong>
             </a>
             - Apple Frames from from
             <em>
              MacStories
             </em>
             ' Federico Viticci adds frames to screenshots taken with your iPhone, iPad, and Apple Watch and makes them look nicer. It's a favorite that we use often here at
             <em>
              MacRumors
             </em>
             .
            </li>
            <li>
             <a href="https://routinehub.co/shortcut/663/">
              <strong>
               Dictate to Notes
              </strong>
             </a>
             - With Dictate to Notes, you can use voice dictation to create a note in the Notes app, which is useful for jotting down quick thoughts without having to type something out.
            </li>
            <li>
             <a href="https://routinehub.co/shortcut/6622/">
              <strong>
               YouTube PiP
              </strong>
             </a>
             - If you want to be able to watch YouTube in Picture in Picture mode on the iPhone, this is the app for you. With an app called
             <a href="https://apps.apple.com/us/app/scriptable/id1405459188">
              Scriptable
             </a>
             , when you run YouTube PiP through the Share Sheet, it will open a YouTube video in a floating window.
            </li>
            <li>
             <a href="https://routinehub.co/shortcut/7290/">
              <strong>
               Music Finder
              </strong>
             </a>
             - To identify a song that's playing nearby you can use Shazam, but Shazam saves music to Apple Music, which is not ideal if you're a Spotify user. Music Finder identifies a song and saves it to your Spotify playlist.
            </li>
            <li>
             <a href="https://www.icloud.com/shortcuts/c9ddf062fead4fe89850fb16b406b62c">
              <strong>
               Set AirPlay
              </strong>
             </a>
             - Set AirPlay makes it easier to swap between your iPhone and your other AirPlay devices, saving you a few taps if you want to switch sources quickly.
            </li>
            <li>
             <a href="https://www.icloud.com/shortcuts/0c06d1131960494f91b5d35896d5cedf">
              <strong>
               Url Shortener
              </strong>
             </a>
             - URL Shortener makes long and unsightly URLs shorter, which is useful when you need to share a naked URL. It lives in the Share Sheet, so all you have to do is select the Shorten URL option when viewing a website and it will generate a short URL. Alternatively, you can copy a link and run it from the Shortcuts app, which will shorten the last copied URL.
            </li>
           </ul>
           <p>
            Do you have a favorite Shortcut? Let us know in the comments and we may feature it in a future video.
           </p>
          </div>
          <div class="desktopExpandWrap--197SeUpp js-expandWrap">
           <a class="button button--2VOdSzvH js-teaseTrigger" href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/19/handy-iphone-shortcuts/">
            Show Full Article
           </a>
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>

           <div class="tShare--2sClpP_C">
