       <article class="article--2pJwZBkO js-article front--3uTQDaAu f_front" expanded="false">
        <div class="titlebar--3N4MCKxL">
         <h2 class="heading--1cooZo6n heading--h5--3l5xQ3lN heading--white--2vAPsAl1 heading--noMargin--mnRHPAnD">
          <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/review/sonnet-egpu-breakaway-pucks/">
           Review: Sonnet's Latest eGPU Breakaway Pucks Give Your Intel Mac a Graphics Boost and Extra Connectivity
          </a>
         </h2>
        </div>
        <div class="byline--3Eec5bcq">
         <time datetime="2021-03-19T12:09:45-07:00">
          Friday March 19, 2021 12:09 pm PDT
         </time>
         by
         <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/author/eric-slivka/" rel="author">
          Eric Slivka
         </a>
        </div>
        <div class="content--2u3grYDr js-content">
         <div class="ugc--2nTu61bm minor--3O_9dH4U" data-io-article-url="https://www.macrumors.com/review/sonnet-egpu-breakaway-pucks/">
          <div class="js-contentInner">
           <p>
            Back in January, Sonnet announced
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/01/06/sonnet-announces-egpu-docks-with-amd-radeon/">
             updated versions of its eGPU Breakaway Pucks
            </a>
            , offering
            <a href="https://www.sonnettech.com/product/egpu-breakaway-puck/overview.html">
             new options equipped with Radeon RX 5500 XT and RX 5700 graphics processors
            </a>
            for Intel-based Macs. The docks connect to a host Mac over Thunderbolt 3 and allow for more powerful graphics capabilities than the included graphics in many Macs while also providing some dock capabilities such as additional USB ports and display connections.
           </p>
           <p>
            <img alt="sonnet pucks" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-789186 lazyload" data-sizes="auto" data-src="https://images.macrumors.com/t/zpuQ6Hm53B0UeSZ8VrEK0BKaiYs=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/sonnet-pucks.jpg?lossy" data-srcset="https://images.macrumors.com/t/zpuQ6Hm53B0UeSZ8VrEK0BKaiYs=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/sonnet-pucks.jpg?lossy 400w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/RCLnxOyugfVEwmbJHAmrBxqQciw=/800x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/sonnet-pucks.jpg?lossy 800w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/X7JEWauJ3AwRxHQsuhROiCkRHcs=/1600x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/sonnet-pucks.jpg 1600w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/VS8IeT2VcgIK7wXZdr32muTli0Y=/2500x0/filters:no_upscale():quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/sonnet-pucks.jpg 2500w" height="898" src="https://images.macrumors.com/images-new/1x1.trans.gif" width="1600"/>
            <noscript>
             <img alt="sonnet pucks" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-789186" height="898" src="https://images.macrumors.com/article-new/2021/03/sonnet-pucks.jpg" width="1600"/>
            </noscript>
            <br/>
            I've been testing out both versions of the Breakaway Puck for a few weeks now, and I've found that they do offer significantly better graphics performance, particularly if you're using an older machine like the 2016 15-inch MacBook Pro with Radeon Pro 450 graphics that I use as my main machine.
           </p>
           <p>
            Both models of the eGPU Breakaway Puck have the same design, featuring a metal enclosure with perforations on the top, front, and sides to help ventilate the dock, which can get quite hot during heavy usage. A large fan is designed to exhaust heat out through the top of the dock, and it will cycle on and off as needed.
           </p>
           <p>
            <img alt="sonnet puck front" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-789187 lazyload" data-sizes="auto" data-src="https://images.macrumors.com/t/UbhbsDgfSxgLFn_6JQCBfn5J_uM=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/sonnet-puck-front.jpg?lossy" data-srcset="https://images.macrumors.com/t/UbhbsDgfSxgLFn_6JQCBfn5J_uM=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/sonnet-puck-front.jpg?lossy 400w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/VeOQqt1lXbbYVURDKJ1gKHEG2g4=/800x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/sonnet-puck-front.jpg?lossy 800w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/Sy9X77RutfMKTbe8By3jNm9gBgA=/1600x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/sonnet-puck-front.jpg 1600w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/qOov0WPZdbG8pno8tBt5PaEqwqI=/2500x0/filters:no_upscale():quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/sonnet-puck-front.jpg 2500w" height="836" src="https://images.macrumors.com/images-new/1x1.trans.gif" width="1600"/>
            <noscript>
             <img alt="sonnet puck front" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-789187" height="836" src="https://images.macrumors.com/article-new/2021/03/sonnet-puck-front.jpg" width="1600"/>
            </noscript>
            <br/>
            The docks measure in at about 6 inches by 5 inches and about 2 inches high, so a bit larger than some standard Thunderbolt 3 docks like my favored CalDigit TS3 Plus, but the Sonnet docks of course come with eGPU capabilities and the large fan that require a larger size. It's still a pretty compact design that fits well on a desk.
           </p>
           <p>
            The overall look is pretty unobtrusive with the black metal and fairly small branding with the company and product name. The most distinctive design element is a wavy blue light on the top of the dock that gives it a bit of a splash and lets you know that it's powered up and connected to a computer.
           </p>
           <p>
            <img alt="sonnet puck mac" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-789188 lazyload" data-sizes="auto" data-src="https://images.macrumors.com/t/RDi9dEF-5U-tZd7MNh4RNYyjoSU=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/sonnet-puck-mac.jpg?lossy" data-srcset="https://images.macrumors.com/t/RDi9dEF-5U-tZd7MNh4RNYyjoSU=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/sonnet-puck-mac.jpg?lossy 400w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/RvVdf_75Zb1oymtdQUGP25nawTA=/800x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/sonnet-puck-mac.jpg?lossy 800w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/o3NjTYVpTrOYhiPycBa-7VgesFk=/1600x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/sonnet-puck-mac.jpg 1600w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/0lGBmr34f5_04BvB9GUeYIrlqik=/2500x0/filters:no_upscale():quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/sonnet-puck-mac.jpg 2500w" height="901" src="https://images.macrumors.com/images-new/1x1.trans.gif" width="1600"/>
            <noscript>
             <img alt="sonnet puck mac" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-789188" height="901" src="https://images.macrumors.com/article-new/2021/03/sonnet-puck-mac.jpg" width="1600"/>
            </noscript>
            <br/>
            The Radeon RX 5500 XT version comes with 4GB of GDDR6 video memory, while the Radeon RX 5700 model comes with 8GB.
           </p>
           <p>
            To quantitatively assess the eGPU performance, I ran several benchmarks using both my machine's built-in graphics and the Breakaway Pucks, and I unsurprisingly found significant improvements when using the eGPU.
           </p>
           <p>
            For my first test, I used Geekbench 5's Compute Benchmark, which rang up Metal scores of averaging 12,085 over three runs using the built-in discrete graphics on my MacBook Pro. Scores improved substantially when I added Sonnet's Breakaway Puck to my system, with the 5500 XT yielding Metal scores averaging 41,595 and the 5700 averaging 56,249. As a point of comparison, I also ran the test on an
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/guide/m1/">
             M1
            </a>
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/roundup/macbook-air/">
             MacBook Air
            </a>
            with 7-core GPU, and that came in with an average score of 18,828.
           </p>
           <p>
            <img alt="geekbench" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-789685 lazyload" data-sizes="auto" data-src="https://images.macrumors.com/t/SDRzcqVTLdJtySDF9M9ImlRezwQ=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/geekbench.jpg?lossy" data-srcset="https://images.macrumors.com/t/SDRzcqVTLdJtySDF9M9ImlRezwQ=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/geekbench.jpg?lossy 400w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/zvH2y7ymLg3VlYgFfjOibljkDw0=/800x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/geekbench.jpg?lossy 800w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/0ugEenxvij3y2_9uAnLm2UL7_fw=/1600x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/geekbench.jpg 1600w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/Ir-UTqhucCPp505MJD2dOdREYfM=/2500x0/filters:no_upscale():quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/geekbench.jpg 2500w" height="520" src="https://images.macrumors.com/images-new/1x1.trans.gif" width="1860"/>
            <noscript>
             <img alt="geekbench" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-789685" height="520" src="https://images.macrumors.com/article-new/2021/03/geekbench.jpg" width="1860"/>
            </noscript>
            <br/>
            My next set of tests came from the GFXBench Metal suite of benchmarking tools, and I similarly found massively improved frame rates in several popular offscreen benchmark tests, again averaged over three runs for each test. In all three benchmarks, the 5500 XT Breakaway Puck delivered approximately four times as many frames per second as my MacBook Pro did on its own, while the 5700 XT puck's advantage was more like five to six times. As with the Geekbench tests, the M1 MacBook Air came in somewhere in the middle.
           </p>
           <p>
            <img alt="gfxbench" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-789686 lazyload" data-sizes="auto" data-src="https://images.macrumors.com/t/CRgnDENvMo6ZSa-KI4LBRgJ-1Zs=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/gfxbench.jpg?lossy" data-srcset="https://images.macrumors.com/t/CRgnDENvMo6ZSa-KI4LBRgJ-1Zs=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/gfxbench.jpg?lossy 400w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/Ya3cG3_4ULS-DZsuBUlDZRTpvQw=/800x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/gfxbench.jpg?lossy 800w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/0z3d9oEPe7CaUHG-phPOFDnr0jw=/1600x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/gfxbench.jpg 1600w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/CdJUzoIay9yqAnu4zoEviQzMipY=/2500x0/filters:no_upscale():quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/gfxbench.jpg 2500w" height="1720" src="https://images.macrumors.com/images-new/1x1.trans.gif" width="1860"/>
            <noscript>
             <img alt="gfxbench" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-789686" height="1720" src="https://images.macrumors.com/article-new/2021/03/gfxbench.jpg" width="1860"/>
            </noscript>
            <br/>
            My final set of tests involved some rendering using DaVinci Resolve. My test footage was a nearly 11-minute 4K clip that I rendered without any additional processing to 1080p using several different codecs: H.264, Apple ProRes 422, and Apple ProRes 422 HQ.
           </p>
           <p>
            These tests are where things started to get a bit more interesting, as while both pucks cut render times by more than half compared to my MacBook Pro running on its own, the results for the two pucks were very similar and in some cases, the 5500 XT GPU performed better than the 5700 GPU.
           </p>
           <p>
            With DaVinci Resolve also having just been updated with Apple silicon support, I was also able to run the tests on my M1 MacBook Air, where I once again found intermediate performance, which is quite impressive for a low-end consumer machine using Apple's first effort at a custom Mac chip, and it'll be very interesting to see how much Apple can improve performance on upcoming M-series chips aimed at more powerful Macs.
           </p>
           <p>
            <img alt="davinci" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-789687 lazyload" data-sizes="auto" data-src="https://images.macrumors.com/t/IIFbX0zwMX5Dzzu0r1dEZwbxpms=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/davinci.jpg?lossy" data-srcset="https://images.macrumors.com/t/IIFbX0zwMX5Dzzu0r1dEZwbxpms=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/davinci.jpg?lossy 400w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/BHPf82Qb4FsJ_bLd9IOdh49z2o8=/800x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/davinci.jpg?lossy 800w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/GO_sBcI23kuUEL9aZdRaeve-fJg=/1600x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/davinci.jpg 1600w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/nldq2KYm3SCZ-nZfGhpmJAyWuhk=/2500x0/filters:no_upscale():quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/davinci.jpg 2500w" height="1620" src="https://images.macrumors.com/images-new/1x1.trans.gif" width="1860"/>
            <noscript>
             <img alt="davinci" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-789687" height="1620" src="https://images.macrumors.com/article-new/2021/03/davinci.jpg" width="1860"/>
            </noscript>
            <br/>
            I talked with the folks at Sonnet about my results and my observations that the renders were not making full use of the eGPUs' capabilities over the course of each run, starting out at nearly 100% but tailing off toward 70% or less after a minute or so.
           </p>
           <p>
            Sonnet's engineering team concluded that it appeared the rest of my MacBook Pro's hardware was a limiting factor in my tests, as even when using an eGPU, the CPU and other components like system memory can become performance bottlenecks. In those cases, the eGPU ends up being at the mercy of thermal throttling or other constraints of the host system and unable to reach peak speeds.
           </p>
           <p>
            For that reason, it's worth highlighting that, at least for my MacBook Pro, the very similar performance between the two eGPUs means that for certain tasks the 5500 XT puck performs just as well as the more expensive 5700 puck, so that's something you might want to consider if you're weighing a purchase.
           </p>
           <p>
            Moving on to the dock capabilities of the pucks, you won't see the breadth of port options available on some regular Thunderbolt docks, but they do give you some decent expansion options. Displays are obviously a big feature for docks to support, and Sonnet's pucks come equipped with a downstream Thunderbolt 3 port, a DisplayPort 1.4 port, and an HDMI 2.0b port for maximum connectivity.
           </p>
           <p>
            <img alt="sonnet puck rear" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-789189 lazyload" data-sizes="auto" data-src="https://images.macrumors.com/t/uUUXIkqlqOkyTqDM460bQODmqkM=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/sonnet-puck-rear.jpg?lossy" data-srcset="https://images.macrumors.com/t/uUUXIkqlqOkyTqDM460bQODmqkM=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/sonnet-puck-rear.jpg?lossy 400w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/6xn0KtFORIW9KuvgjFlLQIe02Wo=/800x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/sonnet-puck-rear.jpg?lossy 800w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/udwFqSnac-P-Fo-kDABLjwA-Aig=/1600x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/sonnet-puck-rear.jpg 1600w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/ccbeVSMHQx3bPrJnVEFXxP9xdXk=/2500x0/filters:no_upscale():quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/sonnet-puck-rear.jpg 2500w" height="742" src="https://images.macrumors.com/images-new/1x1.trans.gif" width="1600"/>
            <noscript>
             <img alt="sonnet puck rear" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-789189" height="742" src="https://images.macrumors.com/article-new/2021/03/sonnet-puck-rear.jpg" width="1600"/>
            </noscript>
            <br/>
            4K and 5K displays, and even Apple's 6K Pro Display XDR, are all compatible with the Breakaway Puck, and I tested things out with an LG UltraFine 5K display and had no issues. The puck can support up to four 4K displays simultaneously if you take advantage of the DisplayPort and HDMI ports and then use a Thunderbolt 3 to Dual DisplayPort or Dual HDMI adapter.
           </p>
           <p>
            It would be nice to see a few other port options like Ethernet or some additional USB-C ports, but at least the two 5 Gbps USB-A ports support a broad range of peripherals. The dock can supply up to 60 watts of power to a host computer, which may not be quite enough if you've got a more powerful machine like a 15-inch or 16-inch MacBook Pro, so you may have to connect a separate power adapter.
           </p>
           <p>
            The fan on the Breakaway Puck does put out a decent bit of noise, so if you're used to a quiet work environment it will definitely be noticeable as it cycles on and off, particularly if it's placed prominently on your desk.
           </p>
           <p>
            For power users who really need the GPU horsepower these Breakaway Pucks can provide, they are a solid addition in a space-saving and even portable design. With souped-up graphics capabilities, display connectivity, and some additional USB expansion, they are good options that can pay for themselves if you're a professional user looking to speed up graphics-intensive tasks. Most consumers will not, however, have a need for this additional hardware.
           </p>
           <p>
            It would be nice to see some even newer and higher-end GPU options in these pucks, but it no doubt takes time to get them integrated into these dock designs, and there's undoubtedly also some effort by Sonnet to target a balance between price and power that will result in the broadest appeal for these accessories.
           </p>
           <p>
            Of course, things become murkier looking toward the future, as Apple's latest Macs based on Apple silicon don't support eGPUs. But there are still plenty of Intel-based Macs out there, so Mac eGPU solutions like Sonnet's Breakaway Pucks will have a market for some time to come.
           </p>
           <p>
            Sonnet's eGPU Breakaway Pucks come bundled with a fairly large external power brick that you'll need to tuck away somewhere and a 0.5-meter Thunderbolt 3 cable. The RX 5500 XT version is priced at $599.99 through
            <a href="https://www.amazon.com/Sonnet-eGPU-Breakaway-Puck-Radeon/dp/B08R15F7B2">
             Amazon
            </a>
            and
            <a href="https://www.sonnetstore.com/collections/egpu-enclosures/products/egpu-breakaway-puck-5500xt">
             Sonnet
            </a>
            , while the RX 5700 version is priced at $899.99 through
            <a href="https://www.amazon.com/Sonnet-eGPU-Breakaway-Puck-Radeon/dp/B08R17T93F">
             Amazon
            </a>
            and
            <a href="https://www.sonnetstore.com/collections/egpu-enclosures/products/egpu-breakaway-puck-5700">
             Sonnet
            </a>
            .
           </p>
           <p>
            <small>
             <em>
              Note: Sonnet provided MacRumors with the Breakaway Pucks on loan for the purpose of this review. No other compensation was received.
             </em>
            </small>
           </p>
           <div class="linkback">

            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/guide/thunderbolt-3/">
             Thunderbolt 3
            </a>
            ,
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/guide/sonnet/">
             Sonnet
            </a>
           </div>

       <article class="article--2pJwZBkO js-article front--3uTQDaAu f_front" expanded="false">
        <div class="titlebar--3N4MCKxL">
         <h2 class="heading--1cooZo6n heading--h5--3l5xQ3lN heading--white--2vAPsAl1 heading--noMargin--mnRHPAnD">
          <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/19/macrumors-giveaway-ipad-pro-amadine/">
           MacRumors Giveaway: Win an 11-Inch iPad Pro and Apple Pencil 2 From Amadine
          </a>
         </h2>
        </div>
        <div class="byline--3Eec5bcq">
         <time datetime="2021-03-19T11:01:54-07:00">
          Friday March 19, 2021 11:01 am PDT
         </time>
         by
         <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/author/juli-clover/" rel="author">
          Juli Clover
         </a>
        </div>
        <div class="content--2u3grYDr js-content">
         <div class="ugc--2nTu61bm minor--3O_9dH4U" data-io-article-url="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/19/macrumors-giveaway-ipad-pro-amadine/">
          <div class="js-contentInner">
           <p>
            For this week's giveaway, we've teamed up with
            <a href="https://amadine.com">
             Amadine
            </a>
            maker Belight Software to offer
            <em>
             MacRumors
            </em>
            readers a chance to win an 11-inch iPad Pro and an Apple Pencil 2, the perfect hardware combination for use with
            <a href="https://apps.apple.com/us/app/amadine/id1339199390">
             the Amadine app
            </a>
            .
           </p>
           <p>
           </p>
           <div class="center-wrap">
            <div class="video-wrapper">
             <div class="video-container">
              <div class="ls_video_embed aspect-16-9 lazyload" data-thumb-size="maxresdefault" data-youtube="fVjg1kuNnqM" data-ytparams="modestbranding=1">
               <button class="play-btn">
                play
               </button>
              </div>
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>
           <br/>
           For those unfamiliar with
           <a href="https://amadine.com">
            Amadine
           </a>
           , it's a vector drawing and illustration app that's available for the iPhone, iPad, and Mac. Amadine is designed with an intuitive, easy to understand interface that makes vector graphic work accessible to beginners and more experienced artists alike. It has all of the features of the
           <a href="https://amadine.com">
            Amadine Mac app
           </a>
           , but has been optimized for a touch and Apple Pencil experience.
           <p>
            <img alt="amadine ipad 1" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-789459 lazyload" data-sizes="auto" data-src="https://images.macrumors.com/t/YBdBgxszMPJdOUyz_wvFj3jxXtY=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/amadine-ipad-1.jpg?lossy" data-srcset="https://images.macrumors.com/t/YBdBgxszMPJdOUyz_wvFj3jxXtY=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/amadine-ipad-1.jpg?lossy 400w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/JQAHEWiYKhnlIlUswL8jGPh-7xY=/800x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/amadine-ipad-1.jpg?lossy 800w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/UvP-mnKhExjdhgVMrb8JAMza_tQ=/1600x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/amadine-ipad-1.jpg 1600w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/FbejWxTK0bem7ynf2kOchosWxIs=/2500x0/filters:no_upscale():quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/amadine-ipad-1.jpg 2500w" height="1333" src="https://images.macrumors.com/images-new/1x1.trans.gif" width="2000"/>
            <noscript>
             <img alt="amadine ipad 1" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-789459" height="1333" src="https://images.macrumors.com/article-new/2021/03/amadine-ipad-1.jpg" width="2000"/>
            </noscript>
            <br/>
            If you've never drawn in an iPad app before, Amadine is straightforward enough that you can spend 10 minutes learning the tools and then have enough knowledge to create simple graphics and eventually, more complex works of art.
           </p>
           <p>
            <img alt="amadine ipad 2" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-789460 lazyload" data-sizes="auto" data-src="https://images.macrumors.com/t/Fi5u6dO5ky6W-XQ44eoopCftTiY=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/amadine-ipad-2.jpg?lossy" data-srcset="https://images.macrumors.com/t/Fi5u6dO5ky6W-XQ44eoopCftTiY=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/amadine-ipad-2.jpg?lossy 400w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/cJc5ws465cu3AH3iQsOwWqtvFWM=/800x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/amadine-ipad-2.jpg?lossy 800w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/ZctUdg9oQ9MzGyQGJV2n2XXVBAo=/1600x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/amadine-ipad-2.jpg 1600w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/Rcl1SuBZhqTl6C_ppFxqlaEmwak=/2500x0/filters:no_upscale():quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/amadine-ipad-2.jpg 2500w" height="1333" src="https://images.macrumors.com/images-new/1x1.trans.gif" width="2000"/>
            <noscript>
             <img alt="amadine ipad 2" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-789460" height="1333" src="https://images.macrumors.com/article-new/2021/03/amadine-ipad-2.jpg" width="2000"/>
            </noscript>
            <br/>
            There's a Quick Start Guide that lets you jump right in with gesture tutorials, a series of videos that teach you how to use the tools, and an online help interface for when you need assistance.
           </p>
           <p>
            Amadine works seamlessly with the Apple Pencil on all compatible iPad models, with support for pressure sensitivity. All of the tools you might need for creating vector art and illustrations are included.
           </p>
           <p>
            <img alt="amadine ipad 4" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-789462 lazyload" data-sizes="auto" data-src="https://images.macrumors.com/t/DzNpZ8hPFKiflewJv8AiUEqMBjM=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/amadine-ipad-4.jpg?lossy" data-srcset="https://images.macrumors.com/t/DzNpZ8hPFKiflewJv8AiUEqMBjM=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/amadine-ipad-4.jpg?lossy 400w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/0baI2pkgKZBr0ydjLzxJyhZlEEI=/800x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/amadine-ipad-4.jpg?lossy 800w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/xXDjfR9bekVaGzlDfJqZsbOPEzc=/1600x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/amadine-ipad-4.jpg 1600w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/0dfXducrOay4ICHvFbBySyJkits=/2500x0/filters:no_upscale():quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/amadine-ipad-4.jpg 2500w" height="1333" src="https://images.macrumors.com/images-new/1x1.trans.gif" width="2000"/>
            <noscript>
             <img alt="amadine ipad 4" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-789462" height="1333" src="https://images.macrumors.com/article-new/2021/03/amadine-ipad-4.jpg" width="2000"/>
            </noscript>
            <br/>
            There are more than 30 vector design tools for drawing, editing, slicing, and typing, including the Pen tool for precision-driven curve creation. You can add multiple strokes and fills with stroke profiles available, and text can be included along a path or inside a shape.
           </p>
           <p>
            <img alt="amadine ipad 3" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-789461 lazyload" data-sizes="auto" data-src="https://images.macrumors.com/t/sni-Q_JC1lW8BaPdv7QWfAEgKis=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/amadine-ipad-3.jpg?lossy" data-srcset="https://images.macrumors.com/t/sni-Q_JC1lW8BaPdv7QWfAEgKis=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/amadine-ipad-3.jpg?lossy 400w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/p0f6gVA4pue1IrSd03nnwPhzc-8=/800x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/amadine-ipad-3.jpg?lossy 800w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/yUu2dqflvbfmEJxtBTNtt_ZznRg=/1600x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/amadine-ipad-3.jpg 1600w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/eVWfwvndtcr26cCGfpmPuxkfXdo=/2500x0/filters:no_upscale():quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/amadine-ipad-3.jpg 2500w" height="1333" src="https://images.macrumors.com/images-new/1x1.trans.gif" width="2000"/>
            <noscript>
             <img alt="amadine ipad 3" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-789461" height="1333" src="https://images.macrumors.com/article-new/2021/03/amadine-ipad-3.jpg" width="2000"/>
            </noscript>
            <br/>
            Paths can be added using the Path and Draw tools, with options to add, remove, and rearrange anchor points. Points can be converted to corner points and smooth points, plus there are Knife, Scissor, and Eraser tools for editing paths and shapes. All paths and shapes can use multiple strokes, fills, and gradients.
           </p>
           <p>
            <img alt="amadine ipad 5" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-789464 lazyload" data-sizes="auto" data-src="https://images.macrumors.com/t/POd2YI6bX8SMjOtc3Ipv5rLHTx4=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/amadine-ipad-5.jpg?lossy" data-srcset="https://images.macrumors.com/t/POd2YI6bX8SMjOtc3Ipv5rLHTx4=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/amadine-ipad-5.jpg?lossy 400w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/CBR9zJvzsuYM4rM2rw2PJRP2PqA=/800x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/amadine-ipad-5.jpg?lossy 800w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/-N7pq39v1wo0dhjUUxu9eCBtVCk=/1600x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/amadine-ipad-5.jpg 1600w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/LS1G2irfZYOEPcE3z0XUiWMkPxA=/2500x0/filters:no_upscale():quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/amadine-ipad-5.jpg 2500w" height="1333" src="https://images.macrumors.com/images-new/1x1.trans.gif" width="2000"/>
            <noscript>
             <img alt="amadine ipad 5" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-789464" height="1333" src="https://images.macrumors.com/article-new/2021/03/amadine-ipad-5.jpg" width="2000"/>
            </noscript>
            <br/>
            With the draw tool, users can take advantage of the Brushes built into the app to use with the freehand Pencil tool for creating smooth vector lines. The Width tool allows for the creation of unique strokes that can be used in drawings, and there are graphics effects options like Inner Glow, Outer Glow, Shadow, and Blur to add depth and style.
           </p>
           <p>
            Amadine is
            <a href="https://apps.apple.com/us/app/amadine/id1339199390">
             free to download
            </a>
            and the full feature set is available, but the free version is limited to a single document at a time. To work with multiple documents and to share those documents across devices, a one-time $9.99 purchase is required.
           </p>
           <p>
            <img alt="amadine ipad 6" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-789463 lazyload" data-sizes="auto" data-src="https://images.macrumors.com/t/yQ9pdzWc4qLWn2Wcn2a1ylfv0NQ=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/amadine-ipad-6.jpg?lossy" data-srcset="https://images.macrumors.com/t/yQ9pdzWc4qLWn2Wcn2a1ylfv0NQ=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/amadine-ipad-6.jpg?lossy 400w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/3m85TAvX8rEbG0dHIau7y_dCpEo=/800x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/amadine-ipad-6.jpg?lossy 800w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/Af69MlszMvDSNSL8KfuYHRt21WU=/1600x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/amadine-ipad-6.jpg 1600w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/pJKSNTTti-ugl1f825X5c5P11b8=/2500x0/filters:no_upscale():quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/amadine-ipad-6.jpg 2500w" height="1333" src="https://images.macrumors.com/images-new/1x1.trans.gif" width="2000"/>
            <noscript>
             <img alt="amadine ipad 6" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-789463" height="1333" src="https://images.macrumors.com/article-new/2021/03/amadine-ipad-6.jpg" width="2000"/>
            </noscript>
            <br/>
            <a href="https://www.belightsoft.com">
             Belight Software
            </a>
            is providing a 128GB 11-inch iPad Pro and Apple Pencil 2 so one lucky
            <em>
             MacRumors
            </em>
            reader can try out the Amadine iPad app for creating art. To enter to win our giveaway, use the Gleam.io widget below and enter an email address. Email addresses will be used solely for contact purposes to reach the winners and send the prizes. You can earn additional entries by subscribing to our
            <a href="https://my.leadpages.net/leadbox/145ef7173f72a2%3A104a9fa76b46dc/5754903989321728/">

            <a href="https://twitter.com/macrumors">

           </p>

       <article class="article--2pJwZBkO js-article front--3uTQDaAu f_front" expanded="false">
        <div class="titlebar--3N4MCKxL">
         <h2 class="heading--1cooZo6n heading--h5--3l5xQ3lN heading--white--2vAPsAl1 heading--noMargin--mnRHPAnD">
          <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/19/iphone-samsung-oled-display-chip-shortage/">
           iPhone Production May Face Disruptions Due to OLED Display Chip Shortage
          </a>
         </h2>
        </div>
        <div class="byline--3Eec5bcq">
         <time datetime="2021-03-19T08:57:26-07:00">
          Friday March 19, 2021 8:57 am PDT
         </time>
         by
         <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/author/sami-fathi/" rel="author">
          Sami Fathi
         </a>
        </div>
        <div class="content--2u3grYDr js-content">
         <div class="ugc--2nTu61bm minor--3O_9dH4U" data-io-article-url="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/19/iphone-samsung-oled-display-chip-shortage/">
          <div class="js-contentInner">
           <p>
            Due to the impacts on Samsung's production of OLED displays as a result of a global chip shortage,
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/guide/iphone/">
             iPhone
            </a>
            production could be facing disruptions, according to
            <em>
             <a href="https://asia.nikkei.com/Business/Tech/Semiconductors/Samsung-chip-fallout-threatens-smartphone-and-PC-supplies">
              Nikkei Asia
             </a>
            </em>
            .
           </p>
           <p>
            <img alt="iphone12truedepth" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-764739 lazyload" data-sizes="auto" data-src="https://images.macrumors.com/t/YAfkMFbB5kkVjFeU4tc2qdvnkQw=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2019/10/iphone12truedepth.jpg?lossy" data-srcset="https://images.macrumors.com/t/YAfkMFbB5kkVjFeU4tc2qdvnkQw=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2019/10/iphone12truedepth.jpg?lossy 400w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/UbAV1xoZQrW2axDB13aNXJYyBR4=/800x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2019/10/iphone12truedepth.jpg?lossy 800w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/5tqXXuH_8R59lClOLdYMTxUb-Hw=/1600x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2019/10/iphone12truedepth.jpg 1600w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/nQxLVoYsYdMKDLHvxWD6o4rOmzY=/2500x0/filters:no_upscale():quality(90)/article-new/2019/10/iphone12truedepth.jpg 2500w" height="751" src="https://images.macrumors.com/images-new/1x1.trans.gif" width="1100"/>
            <noscript>
             <img alt="iphone12truedepth" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-764739" height="751" src="https://images.macrumors.com/article-new/2019/10/iphone12truedepth.jpg" width="1100"/>
            </noscript>
            <br/>
            Last month, Samsung was forced to shut down its chip fabrication plant in Texas due to large winter storms. The plant is responsible for 5% of the global supply of chips for smartphones and personal computers, and its closure has caused a widespread global shortage. The plant makes chips for Samsung OLED displays, which Apple uses for the iPhone.
           </p>
           <blockquote>
            <p>
             The Samsung Texas plant manufactures telecommunications chips for the U.S. semiconductor giant Qualcomm. The facility also produces chips for organic light-emitting diode panels and for image sensors.
            </p>
            <p>
             The supply crunch hitting Qualcomm will affect a wide range of smartphone makers that rely on the company for key components. Apple, which procures OLED panels from Samsung, could also face disruptions in iPhone production.
            </p>
           </blockquote>
           <p>
            The report doesn't elaborate on the specifics, including which iPhone models would be impacted or the length of the aforementioned disruptions. Last year, due to the global health crisis, Apple suppliers were forced to close factories in China and elsewhere around the world. The closures led to the delayed launch of the
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/roundup/iphone-12/">
             iPhone 12
            </a>
            in October, which typically happens in September.
           </p>
           <p>
            Apple analyst
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/guide/ming-chi-kuo/">
             Ming-Chi Kuo
            </a>
            says, however, that the 2021 iPhone should be
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2020/12/12/kuo-expects-iphone-13-mass-production-on-time/">
             expected in September
            </a>
            , specifically saying that Apple suppliers are poised to begin mass production within Apple's usual summer timeframe.
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2020/09/08/iphone-12-production-sept-airtags-already-started/">
             Reports
            </a>
            last year indicated mass production for the iPhone 12 series did not begin until September.
           </p>
           <div class="linkback">
            Tag:
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/guide/iphone/">
             iPhone Guide
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="desktopExpandWrap--197SeUpp js-expandWrap">

            Show Full Article
           </a>
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>

          </a>

       <article class="article--2pJwZBkO js-article front--3uTQDaAu f_front" expanded="false">
        <div class="titlebar--3N4MCKxL">
         <h2 class="heading--1cooZo6n heading--h5--3l5xQ3lN heading--white--2vAPsAl1 heading--noMargin--mnRHPAnD">
          <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/19/apple-music-scraps-personalized-artwork-stations/">
           Apple Music Scraps Personalized Artwork for Personal Radio Stations
          </a>
         </h2>
        </div>
        <div class="byline--3Eec5bcq">
         <time datetime="2021-03-19T08:41:56-07:00">
          Friday March 19, 2021 8:41 am PDT
         </time>
         by
         <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/author/hartley-charlton/" rel="author">
          Hartley Charlton
         </a>
        </div>
        <div class="content--2u3grYDr js-content">
         <div class="ugc--2nTu61bm minor--3O_9dH4U" data-io-article-url="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/19/apple-music-scraps-personalized-artwork-stations/">
          <div class="js-contentInner">
           <p>
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/guide/apple-music/">
             Apple Music
            </a>
            appears to have removed the personalized artwork for Apple Music's personal radio stations feature, replacing users' artwork with a uniform graphic.
           </p>
           <p>
            <img alt="apple music personal radio stations" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-789850 lazyload" data-sizes="auto" data-src="https://images.macrumors.com/t/ZV-pBFKSsIxF_YdyFGKuSbOJBvY=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/apple-music-personal-radio-stations.jpg?lossy" data-srcset="https://images.macrumors.com/t/ZV-pBFKSsIxF_YdyFGKuSbOJBvY=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/apple-music-personal-radio-stations.jpg?lossy 400w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/gmdchdSELzwj6ttVsq9qqfr5duY=/800x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/apple-music-personal-radio-stations.jpg?lossy 800w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/czOahK7qkJemMTuQNe0x_-I7CQQ=/1600x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/apple-music-personal-radio-stations.jpg 1600w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/tD5IaXgRi43pRgIIYC-687MwcI4=/2500x0/filters:no_upscale():quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/apple-music-personal-radio-stations.jpg 2500w" height="900" src="https://images.macrumors.com/images-new/1x1.trans.gif" width="1600"/>
            <noscript>
             <img alt="apple music personal radio stations" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-789850" height="900" src="https://images.macrumors.com/article-new/2021/03/apple-music-personal-radio-stations.jpg" width="1600"/>
            </noscript>
            <br/>
            Personalized algorithmic radio stations is a popular Apple Music feature that auto-generates a custom radio station for a user based on their listening habits and preferences.
           </p>
           <p>
            Apple Music previously generated a custom personal radio station graphic based on a user's Apple Music profile picture, but Apple now appears to have removed this feature, replacing all personal radio station artwork with an identical red graphic. The change may be in line with a number of amendments to Apple Music's artwork that have taken place
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2020/07/07/apple-music-animated-artwork/">
             over the last year
            </a>
            , such as
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2020/12/11/apple-music-animated-album-artwork/">
             animated album covers
            </a>
            .
           </p>
           <p>
            The change, first spotted by
            <a href="https://www.reddit.com/r/AppleMusic/comments/m83bgp/did_apple_really_remove_the_profile_pictures_out/">
             users on Reddit
            </a>
            , appears to have taken place very recently. Some users seem to be unhappy about the change, commenting that the "profile picture variant made it feel more personal than this." Another downside seems to be that when listening to another user's personal radio station now, the only way to tell who the station is from is by a small profile picture in the bottom right-hand corner, rather than from the artwork itself.
           </p>
           <div class="linkback">
            Tag:
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/guide/apple-music/">
             Apple Music Guide
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="desktopExpandWrap--197SeUpp js-expandWrap">
           <a class="button button--2VOdSzvH js-teaseTrigger" href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/19/apple-music-scraps-personalized-artwork-stations/">
            Show Full Article
           </a>
          </div>
         </div>

        <div class="titlebar--3N4MCKxL">
         <h2 class="heading--1cooZo6n heading--h5--3l5xQ3lN heading--white--2vAPsAl1 heading--noMargin--mnRHPAnD">
          <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/19/deals-pad-quills-winter-sale/">
           Deals: Pad &amp; Quill's Winter Clearance Sale Continues With Up to 50% Off Accessories for iPad, iPhone, and More
          </a>
         </h2>
        </div>
        <div class="byline--3Eec5bcq">
         <time datetime="2021-03-19T08:15:52-07:00">
          Friday March 19, 2021 8:15 am PDT
         </time>
         by
         <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/author/mitchel-broussard/" rel="author">
          Mitchel Broussard
         </a>
        </div>
        <div class="content--2u3grYDr js-content">
         <div class="ugc--2nTu61bm minor--3O_9dH4U" data-io-article-url="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/19/deals-pad-quills-winter-sale/">
          <div class="js-contentInner">
           <p>
            Earlier in the month
            <a href="https://shareasale.com/r.cfm?b=630152&amp;u=63177&amp;m=54540&amp;urllink=www%2Epadandquill%2Ecom%2F&amp;afftrack=">
             Pad &amp; Quill
            </a>
            kicked off a
            <a href="https://shareasale.com/r.cfm?b=630152&amp;u=63177&amp;m=54540&amp;urllink=www%2Epadandquill%2Ecom%2Fpad%2Dquill%2Dholiday%2Dleather%2Dgift%2Dguide%2Ehtml&amp;afftrack=">
             <strong>
              Winter Clearance Sale
             </strong>
            </a>
            , providing 40 to 50 percent off a large collection of accessories on its website. This sale has continued into March, with new items being discounted.
           </p>
           <p>
            <img alt="Pad and Quill Winter Clearance Sale Feature" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-789821 lazyload" data-sizes="auto" data-src="https://images.macrumors.com/t/whsHfI-VPevI9QriatBPHvks26Y=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/Pad-and-Quill-Winter-Clearance-Sale-Feature.jpg?lossy" data-srcset="https://images.macrumors.com/t/whsHfI-VPevI9QriatBPHvks26Y=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/Pad-and-Quill-Winter-Clearance-Sale-Feature.jpg?lossy 400w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/Pmgx_0WzlTPU7dIFo0C3NQ9caa4=/800x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/Pad-and-Quill-Winter-Clearance-Sale-Feature.jpg?lossy 800w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/1KsA77CHuMSGKUzam3TDEHy1uA8=/1600x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/Pad-and-Quill-Winter-Clearance-Sale-Feature.jpg 1600w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/mSenSH4T1qEOqQftw1ZpROH9mME=/2500x0/filters:no_upscale():quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/Pad-and-Quill-Winter-Clearance-Sale-Feature.jpg 2500w" height="1406" src="https://images.macrumors.com/images-new/1x1.trans.gif" width="2500"/>
            <noscript>
             <img alt="Pad and Quill Winter Clearance Sale Feature" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-789821" height="1406" src="https://images.macrumors.com/article-new/2021/03/Pad-and-Quill-Winter-Clearance-Sale-Feature.jpg" width="2500"/>
            </noscript>
            <em>
             <small>
              Note: MacRumors is an affiliate partner with Pad &amp; Quill. When you click a link and make a purchase, we may receive a small payment, which helps us keep the site running.
             </small>
            </em>
           </p>
           <p>
            Pad &amp; Quill is known for its leather cases for iPhone, iPad, and MacBook, and the company also sells Apple Watch bands, wallets, notebooks, and more. Shoppers should note that this sale does not require any special promo code; all of the discount prices you see below have been automatically applied on Pad &amp; Quill's website.
           </p>
           <p>
            Although some of the items that we previously highlighted have now returned to full price, quite a few other items remain at a steep discount on Pad &amp; Quill. Be sure to
            <a href="https://shareasale.com/r.cfm?b=630152&amp;u=63177&amp;m=54540&amp;urllink=www%2Epadandquill%2Ecom%2F&amp;afftrack=">

       <article class="article--2pJwZBkO js-article front--3uTQDaAu f_front" expanded="false">
        <div class="titlebar--3N4MCKxL">
         <h2 class="heading--1cooZo6n heading--h5--3l5xQ3lN heading--white--2vAPsAl1 heading--noMargin--mnRHPAnD">
          <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/19/imac-pro-currently-unavailable-in-us/">
           iMac Pro is Out of Stock Again in U.S. After Being Discontinued
          </a>
         </h2>
        </div>
        <div class="byline--3Eec5bcq">
         <time datetime="2021-03-19T07:31:05-07:00">
          Friday March 19, 2021 7:31 am PDT
         </time>
         by
         <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/author/joe-rossignol/" rel="author">
          Joe Rossignol
         </a>
        </div>
        <div class="content--2u3grYDr js-content">
         <div class="ugc--2nTu61bm minor--3O_9dH4U" data-io-article-url="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/19/imac-pro-currently-unavailable-in-us/">
          <div class="js-contentInner">
           <p>
            Earlier this month, Apple confirmed that the
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/06/apple-confirms-imac-pro-will-be-discontinued/">
             iMac Pro is being discontinued
            </a>
            . The standard configuration of the computer has remained available "while supplies last," but even this configuration is out of stock again in multiple countries.
           </p>
           <p>
            <img alt="iMac Pro Alert Feature" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-787647 lazyload" data-sizes="auto" data-src="https://images.macrumors.com/t/fhna1R9kcHaX6KtiD3OiEjtirtQ=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/iMac-Pro-Alert-Feature.jpg?lossy" data-srcset="https://images.macrumors.com/t/fhna1R9kcHaX6KtiD3OiEjtirtQ=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/iMac-Pro-Alert-Feature.jpg?lossy 400w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/KvHSGt-lw4bLcqVEU5vzw4c_cTQ=/800x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/iMac-Pro-Alert-Feature.jpg?lossy 800w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/-SQtPEgIN_YEYe5lgOk92xKZyJs=/1600x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/iMac-Pro-Alert-Feature.jpg 1600w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/-vdaX1OKIJBx88ZNvzx6hILus0w=/2500x0/filters:no_upscale():quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/iMac-Pro-Alert-Feature.jpg 2500w" height="1268" src="https://images.macrumors.com/images-new/1x1.trans.gif" width="2254"/>
            <noscript>
             <img alt="iMac Pro Alert Feature" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-787647" height="1268" src="https://images.macrumors.com/article-new/2021/03/iMac-Pro-Alert-Feature.jpg" width="2254"/>
            </noscript>
            <br/>
            Apple's online store lists the iMac Pro as
            <a href="https://www.apple.com/shop/buy-mac/imac-pro">
             "Currently Unavailable" in the United States
            </a>
            , Canada, Mexico, Brazil, Australia, Italy, Spain, Portugal, and select other countries. The standard iMac Pro remains available across much of the rest of Europe and Asia, but with lengthy shipping estimates. It's likely that iMac Pro availability will continue to fluctuate, but the end of the line is clearly in sight for the computer.
           </p>
           <p>
            Released in December 2017, the iMac Pro received no substantial hardware refreshes over its lifetime and continues to be sold for $4,999.
           </p>
           <p>
            Apple said the 27-inch iMac introduced in August 2020 has become the preferred choice for the vast majority of pro iMac users. The latest 27-inch iMac configured with a 10-core Core i9 processor is both faster and less expensive than the standard iMac Pro with a 10-core Xeon W processor. Apple said customers who need even more performance and expandability can choose the Mac Pro, released in December 2019.
           </p>
           <p>
            For customers who are still interested in the iMac Pro, Apple recently
            <a href="https://www.apple.com/shop/refurbished/mac/imac-pro">
             added a variety of configurations to its refurbished store
            </a>
            .
           </p>
           <p>
            Apple is rumored to be working on a
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/01/15/apple-redesigned-imacs-slimmer-bezels/">
             redesigned iMac with Apple silicon
            </a>
            for release later this year, so many customers may want to exercise patience. The new iMac's design is said to be inspired by Apple's high-end Pro Display XDR, with a flat back, slimmer bezels around the display, and no metal "chin" below the display.
           </p>
           <div class="linkback">
            Related Roundup:
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/roundup/imac-pro/">
             iMac Pro
            </a>
           </div>
           <div class="linkback">
            Buyer's Guide:
            <a href="https://buyersguide.macrumors.com/#iMac_Pro">
             iMac Pro (Don't Buy)
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>

            Show Full Article
           </a>
          </div>

       <article class="article--2pJwZBkO js-article front--3uTQDaAu f_front" expanded="false">
        <div class="titlebar--3N4MCKxL">
         <h2 class="heading--1cooZo6n heading--h5--3l5xQ3lN heading--white--2vAPsAl1 heading--noMargin--mnRHPAnD">
          <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/19/instagram-for-kids-under-13-in-the-works/">
           Facebook Is Developing a Version of Instagram for Children Under 13
          </a>
         </h2>
        </div>
        <div class="byline--3Eec5bcq">
         <time datetime="2021-03-19T04:22:08-07:00">
          Friday March 19, 2021 4:22 am PDT
         </time>
         by
         <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/author/tim-hardwick/" rel="author">
          Tim Hardwick
         </a>
        </div>
        <div class="content--2u3grYDr js-content">
         <div class="ugc--2nTu61bm minor--3O_9dH4U" data-io-article-url="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/19/instagram-for-kids-under-13-in-the-works/">
          <div class="js-contentInner">
           <p>
            Facebook is developing a version of Instagram thats specifically aimed at children under 13, according to an internal company post (via
            <em>
             <a href="https://www.buzzfeednews.com/article/ryanmac/facebook-instagram-for-children-under-13">
              BuzzFeed News
             </a>
            </em>
            ).
           </p>
           <p>
            <img alt="Instagram Feature 2" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-786418 lazyload" data-sizes="auto" data-src="https://images.macrumors.com/t/3LHkGs_I7a8dNe8Cj8_LWD4Tcyc=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/Instagram-Feature-2.jpg?lossy" data-srcset="https://images.macrumors.com/t/3LHkGs_I7a8dNe8Cj8_LWD4Tcyc=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/Instagram-Feature-2.jpg?lossy 400w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/pDLc_anAZZ43j46Zoc9FBG4ekCE=/800x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/Instagram-Feature-2.jpg?lossy 800w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/0EngJRWNLSPbrrwF7hGVXK02phI=/1600x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/Instagram-Feature-2.jpg 1600w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/fKY2ywbylbBhwimzOcMK9Jul-zE=/2500x0/filters:no_upscale():quality(90)/article-new/2021/03/Instagram-Feature-2.jpg 2500w" height="1266" src="https://images.macrumors.com/images-new/1x1.trans.gif" width="2250"/>
            <noscript>
             <img alt="Instagram Feature 2" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-786418" height="1266" src="https://images.macrumors.com/article-new/2021/03/Instagram-Feature-2.jpg" width="2250"/>
            </noscript>
           </p>
           <blockquote>
            <p>
             "I'm excited to announce that going forward, we have identified youth work as a priority for Instagram and have added it to our H1 priority list," Vishal Shah, Instagram's vice president of product, wrote on an employee message board on Thursday. "We will be building a new youth pillar within the Community Product Group to focus on two things: (a) accelerating our integrity and privacy work to ensure the safest possible experience for teens and (b) building a version of Instagram that allows people under the age of 13 to safely use Instagram for the first time."
            </p>
           </blockquote>
           <p>
            Instagram's policy prohibits kids under 13 from using the platform. Head of Instagram Adam Mosseri later
            <a href="https://twitter.com/mosseri/status/1372691059348631555?s=20">
             confirmed in a tweet
            </a>
            that a version of the popular photo sharing app is "something we're exploring."
           </p>
           <p>
            "Kids are increasingly asking their parents if they can join apps that help them keep up with their friends," wrote Mosseri. "A version of Instagram where parents have control, like we did [with] Messenger Kids, is something we're exploring. We'll share more down the road."
           </p>
           <p>
            The news follows a blog post from Instagram earlier this week in which the Facebook-owned company
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/16/instagram-protecting-young-people-tools/">
             described changes
            </a>
            coming to the platform with the aim of "protecting young people."
           </p>
           <p>
            In the post, Instagram admitted that some young users "can lie about their date of birth," when signing up to the platgform, and said it now asks some new users for a form of age verification, but the post didn't mention its work on a distinct platform specifically for children.
           </p>
           <p>
            In 2017, Facebook
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2017/12/04/facebook-kids-only-messenger/">
             launched
            </a>
            Messenger Kids, which is aimed at children between the ages of 6 and 12. Following the launch, several children's health advocates called on Facebook CEO Mark Zuckerberg to discontinue the product,
            <a href="https://commercialfreechildhood.org/wp-content/uploads/archive/devel-generate/gaw/FBMessengerKids.pdf">
             citing research
            </a>
            that "excessive use of digital devices and social media is harmful to children and teens, making it very likely this new app will undermine children's healthy development."
           </p>
           <p>
            Facebook said it had consulted multiple of experts during the app's development, although a
            <em>
             Wired
            </em>
            report later
            <a href="https://www.wired.com/story/facebook-funds-its-favorite-experts-but-skirts-tough-critics/">
             revealed
            </a>
            that the company had financial relationships with many of the people and organizations that advised on the product.
           </p>
           <p>
            In 2019,
            <em>
             <a href="https://www.theverge.com/2019/7/22/20706250/facebook-messenger-kids-bug-chat-app-unauthorized-adults">
              The Verge
             </a>
            </em>
            reported on a bug in Messenger Kids that allowed children to join groups with strangers. Facebook soon acted to resolve the issue, claiming it had only affected a "small number of group chats."
           </p>
           <div class="linkback">
            Tags:
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/guide/facebook/">
             Facebook
            </a>
            ,
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/guide/instagram/">
             Instagram
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="desktopExpandWrap--197SeUpp js-expandWrap">
           <a class="button button--2VOdSzvH js-teaseTrigger" href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/19/instagram-for-kids-under-13-in-the-works/">
            Show Full Article
           </a>
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>

           <div class="tShare--2sClpP_C">
           </div>

       <article class="article--2pJwZBkO js-article front--3uTQDaAu f_front" expanded="false">
        <div class="titlebar--3N4MCKxL">
         <h2 class="heading--1cooZo6n heading--h5--3l5xQ3lN heading--white--2vAPsAl1 heading--noMargin--mnRHPAnD">
          <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/19/tim-cook-durable-and-hopeful-future-op-ed/">
           Tim Cook Calls for a 'Durable and Hopeful Future For All' in Wall Street Journal Op-Ed
          </a>
         </h2>
        </div>
        <div class="byline--3Eec5bcq">
         <time datetime="2021-03-19T03:12:29-07:00">
          Friday March 19, 2021 3:12 am PDT
         </time>
         by
         <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/author/sami-fathi/" rel="author">
          Sami Fathi
         </a>
        </div>
        <div class="content--2u3grYDr js-content">
         <div class="ugc--2nTu61bm minor--3O_9dH4U" data-io-article-url="https://www.macrumors.com/2021/03/19/tim-cook-durable-and-hopeful-future-op-ed/">
          <div class="js-contentInner">
           <p>
            Apple CEO
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/guide/tim-cook/">
             Tim Cook
            </a>
            has penned an op-ed for the
            <em>
             <a href="https://www.wsj.com/articles/tim-cook-on-the-pandemic-year-the-urgency-of-racial-justice-11616090633">
              Wall Street Journal
             </a>
            </em>
            , calling for more action to be taken against systemic racism and the need to speak up in light of the disproportionate impact that the pandemic has had on communities.
           </p>
           <p>
            <img alt="tim cook interview with cbs 6 20" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-746706 lazyload" data-sizes="auto" data-src="https://images.macrumors.com/t/ARmRpmclAItkAzD6raOL9JgnOHo=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2020/06/tim-cook-interview-with-cbs-6-20.jpg?lossy" data-srcset="https://images.macrumors.com/t/ARmRpmclAItkAzD6raOL9JgnOHo=/400x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2020/06/tim-cook-interview-with-cbs-6-20.jpg?lossy 400w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/TLFbu8ID-ALmAELp0v-lzt8bcvI=/800x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2020/06/tim-cook-interview-with-cbs-6-20.jpg?lossy 800w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/fQxtwFjym0EWZqjkgcFyLECBxBY=/1600x0/filters:quality(90)/article-new/2020/06/tim-cook-interview-with-cbs-6-20.jpg 1600w,https://images.macrumors.com/t/LLiVZM6-XM_-wQUIlUgf96BCwPA=/2500x0/filters:no_upscale():quality(90)/article-new/2020/06/tim-cook-interview-with-cbs-6-20.jpg 2500w" height="700" src="https://images.macrumors.com/images-new/1x1.trans.gif" width="1240"/>
            <noscript>
             <img alt="tim cook interview with cbs 6 20" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-746706" height="700" src="https://images.macrumors.com/article-new/2020/06/tim-cook-interview-with-cbs-6-20.jpg" width="1240"/>
            </noscript>
            <br/>
            Cook's piece highlights how the pandemic has impacted various communities differently and draws on his personal experience of growing up during the civil rights movement.
            <br/>
           </p>
           <blockquote>
            <p>
             In simple theory, a disease should affect all of us equally. But in plain fact, the opposite is true. We have all seen, in real time, how structural discrimination and obstacles to opportunity do their work in a crisis. In our communities, every burdenfrom rates of infection and care outcomes, to economic adversity, to the challenges of virtual learning when schools are closedfalls heaviest on those for whom true equity has always been farthest from reach. As someone who grew up during the civil-rights movement, it has been frustrating to see how much work is still to be done but heartening to see the degree to which people of good will have set aside comfort with the status quo to march and to demand something better.
            </p>
           </blockquote>
           <p>
            As the end of the pandemic nears, Cook says it is a collective responsibility to ensure that moving forward, all individuals, communities, companies, and governments do everything they can to ensure a hopeful and "durable" future for all.
            <br/>
           </p>
           <blockquote>
            <p>
             When the pandemic recedes, we can't simply assume that healing follows. It falls on all of usindividuals and communities, companies and governmentsto ensure that what's ahead is not just the end of a disease but a durable and hopeful future for all who sacrificed and endured during this unprecedented time.
            </p>
           </blockquote>
           <p>
            The global health crisis has forced millions of students to learn remotely from home, and Cook says Apple is committed to building "powerful learning tools and [sharing] them freely with tens of thousands of teachers, educators, and parents." Cook goes on to describe Apple's multiple investments for Black and underrepresented communities.
            <br/>
           </p>
           <blockquote>
            <p>
             And it's led us to undertake major new investments through our Racial Equity and Justice Initiative. These projects include the Propel Center in Atlanta, which we're helping to build in partnership with the country's historically Black colleges and universities, to support the next generation of leaders of color in fields ranging from machine learning to app development, entrepreneurship to design; and our first Apple Developer Academy in the U.S., in downtown Detroit, home to more than 50,000 Black-owned businesses and no shortage of great ideas for the app economy.
            </p>
           </blockquote>
           <p>
            Cook ends with a hopeful message, saying that if anything, he hopes this pandemic has taught us that there is a need to speak up and that a long history of injustice should not be used as an excuse to do nothing.
            <br/>
           </p>
           <blockquote>
            <p>
             The old saying goes that the best time to plant a tree was 20 years ago, but the second best time is today. If this pandemic has taught us anything, I hope its that none of us can use injustices long history as an excuse not to act. Our lives on this planet are precious and fleeting, and fate has a way of reminding us that society is only as strong as those who, for too long, have gone overlooked and undervalued.
            </p>
           </blockquote>
           <p>
            Cook's full op-ed can be read with a subscription to
            <em>
             <a href="https://www.wsj.com/articles/tim-cook-on-the-pandemic-year-the-urgency-of-racial-justice-11616090633">
              The Wall Street Journal
             </a>
            </em>
            .
           </p>
           <p>
            <small>
             Note: Due to the political or social nature of the discussion regarding this topic, the discussion thread is located in our
             <a href="https://forums.macrumors.com/forums/political-news.218/">
              Political News
             </a>
             forum. All forum members and site visitors are welcome to read and follow the thread, but posting is limited to forum members with at least 100 posts.
            </small>
           </p>
           <div class="linkback">

            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/guide/tim-cook/">
             Tim Cook
            </a>
            ,
            <a href="https://www.macrumors.com/guide/racial-equity-and-justice-initiative/">
             Racial Equity and Justice Initiative
            </a>
           </div>
